tena nirbhartsitaiḥ pāpaiḥ kathyamānāṃ kathāṃ śṛṇu  RKS 
rakto mūḍhaś ca loko 'yam akārye saṃpravartate 
na cātmānaṃ vijānāti na paraṃ na ca daivatam  RKS 
na śṛṇoti paraṃ śreyaḥ sati cakṣuṣi nekṣate 
same pathi śanair gacchan plavate sma pade pade  RKS 
evam ukto dharmarājaḥ saṃkṣepāt pāpadehinām 
vistareṇa yadā cakhyau teṣāṃ tac chṛṇu sāmpratam  RKS 
yama uvāca
mayā mukto na jānāti bodhyamāno budhair api 
saṃsāre kliśyate nānā rāgalobhavaśāt naraḥ  RKS 
garbhapātena bhāvena śāstram uktaṃ na budhyate 
narair na śrūyate karma svargamokṣaprasādhakam  RKS 
santapyati śivadhyāne sarvakāmārthasādhane 
narakād ātmanaḥ śreyo yadatra mahadadbhutam  RKS 
pretabhūtā narāḥ sarve yamalokaṃ samāgatāḥ 
ākhyānaṃ kathayiṣyāmi yathoddiṣṭaṃ purātanam  RKS 
sūryeṇa kathitaṃ tv āsīn narmadākhyānam uttamam 
devatānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca mama pitrānukampayā  RKS 
sapādalakṣam adhikaṃ brahmaṇā kathitaṃ raveḥ 
tatra śrutaṃ mayā kṛtsnaṃ brahmaṇā tu śivāc chrutam  RKS 
śivena kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ pārvatyāḥ ṣaṇmukhasya tu 
jambūdvīpaṃ samāsādya mānuṣīṃ yonim āśritaḥ  RKS 
nāśrayennarmadāṃ devīṃ saptakalpavahāṃ tu yaḥ 
snānāvagāhanāt pānāt tathā dānakriyādibhiḥ  RKS 
loke 'smin gatidā kānyā pāpopahatacetasām 
ye dhyāyanti mahādevīṃ narmadāṃ pāpahāriṇīm  RKS 
aghāni teṣāṃ naśyanti tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā 
narmadāṃ saṃsmared yas tu kīrtayed yas tu vā girā  RKS 
paralokaṃ samāyāto yamadūtair na bādhyate 
narmadāṃ kīrtayed yas tu pāpakarmā narādhamaḥ  RKS 
narakān samayoddiṣṭān na ca krāmati karhicit 
gaṅgādyāḥ saritastatra tīrthakoṭir anekadhā  RKS 
revātejaḥ pratāpena śuddhiṃ gacchanti tatkṣaṇāt 
narakasthaḥ smared yas tu mekalāṃ tu haraṃ harim  RKS 
mucyate yamadūtaiḥ sa tatkṣaṇān nātra saṃśayaḥ 
yadi tiṣṭhati vaidūryaparvate 'marakaṇṭake  RKS 
oṃkāraḥ parameśāno bhuktimuktiphalapradaḥ 
kimarthaṃ tv iha śocanti pāpopahatacetasaḥ  RKS 
siddheśvaraṃ siddhaliṅgaṃ lokānugrahakārakam 
yajñeśvaraṃ ca madhye tu tatraiva śaśibhūṣaṇam  RKS 
narmadā dakṣiṇe bhāge liṅgaṃ caiva maheśvaram 
caturthaṃ kapileśaṃ ca śivakṣetraṃ vidurbudhāḥ  RKS 
ye 'rcayanti sadā bhaktyā puṣpadhūpārtitarpaṇaiḥ 
śivalokaṃ tu te yānti narakān nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKS 
etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ yathā pṛṣṭaṃ tvayānagha 
pāpiṣṭhān nṝnadharmasthān kathayāmāsa bhārata  
steht so dort
godānaṃ hemadānaṃ ca tiladānaṃ tathaiva ca 
annadānaṃ payodānaṃ sarvopaskaram eva ca  RKS 
prāsādārāmadānaṃ ca ye kurvanti narottamāḥ 
yamalokaṃ na te yānti narakaṃ ghorarūpiṇam  RKS 
mucyante sarvapāpebhyaḥ śivasya vacanaṃ yathā 
sanmānaṃ cāpamānena viyogeneṣṭasaṅgamam  RKS 
yauvanaṃ jarayā grastaṃ kaṣṭāt saukhyamupadrutam 
valibhiḥ palitaiś cāpi jarjarīkṛtavigrahaḥ  RKS 
kiṃ karoti naraḥ prājño jarayā jarjarīkṛtaḥ 
strīpuṃsor yauvanaṃ rūpaṃ yadanyo 'nyaṃ priyaṃkaram  RKS 
tad eva jarayā grastam ubhayor api na priyam 
apūrvavat tathātmānaṃ śaithilyena samanvitam  RKS 
yaḥ paśyan na virajyeta ko 'nyas tasmād acetanaḥ 
jarābhibhūtaḥ puruṣaḥ patnīputrādibāndhavaiḥ  RKS 
aśaktatvād durācārair bhṛtyaiś ca paribhūyate 
dharmam arthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca mokṣaṃ na jarayā yutaḥ  RKS 
śaktaḥ sādhayituṃ tasmāt purā dharmaṃ samācaret 
vātapittakaphādīnāṃ vaiṣamyaṃ ca yudhiṣṭhira  RKS 
vātādīnāṃ samūhaś ca dehajaḥ parikīrtitaḥ 
tasmād vyādhiparaṃ jñeyaṃ śarīram idam ātmanaḥ  RKS 
vātotpatty atirekeṇa bādhito vai jvareṇa ca 
rogair nānāvidhibhavair bahuduḥkhāny anekadhā  RKS 
tāni ca svātmavedyāni kim anyat kathayāmy aham 
ekottaraṃ mṛtyuśatam asmin dehe pratiṣṭhitam  RKS 
atraikaṃ kālarūpaṃ ca śeṣāstvāgantavaḥ smṛtāḥ 
ye tv ihāgantavaḥ proktāste praśāmyanti bhaiṣajaiḥ  RKS 
japahomapradānaiś ca kālamṛtyur na śāmyati 
apamṛtyuś ca sarvasya viṣam adyādisambhavaḥ  RKS 
na cātipuruṣas tasmād apamṛtyor babheti vai 
vividhā vyādhayaḥ kaṣṭāḥ savaidyāḥ prāṇinas tathā  RKS 
viṣāṇi tv abhicārāś ca mṛtyor dvārāṇi dehinām 
pīḍitaṃ rogasarpādyair api dhanvantariḥ svayam  RKS 
svasthaṃ kartuṃ na śaknoti kālaprāptaṃ hi dehinam 
naiṣadhaṃ na tapo dānaṃ na mitrāṇi na bāndhavāḥ  RKS 
paritrātuṃ no samarthāḥ kālena paripīḍitam 
nāsti mṛtyusamaṃ duḥkhaṃ nāsti mṛtyusamo ripuḥ  RKS 
nāsti mṛtyusamaḥ kālaḥ sarveṣām eva dehinām 
sadbhāryā putramitrāṇi rājyaiśvaryasukhāni ca  RKS 
mṛtyuśchinatti sarvāṇi vividhāny api bhārata 
idaṃ te kathitaṃ rājañjñātisaṃsāradustaram  RKS 
pariṇāma iti jñātvā sarvaṅkālasya bhojanam 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena saṃsevyā saptakalpagā  RKS 
sarvaduḥkhāpahā nityaṃ sarvaśokavināśinī 
yo yān kāmayate kāmāṃstāṃstān devī prayacchati  RKS 
idaṃ jñānam idaṃ dhyānaṃ pāṇḍityaṃ veda vedanam 
nivāsaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sevyate saptakalpagā  RKS 
yajño dānaṃ tapaḥ satyaṃ svādhyāyaḥ pitṛtarpaṇam 
saphalaṃ labhate teṣāṃ yo revāmbu niṣevate  RKS 
brahmakūrcasahasrāṇi somapānāyutaṃ tathā 
narmadātoyapānasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm  RKS 
saṃyukto 'pi mahāpāpair nānājanmakṛtair api 
oṃkāradakṣiṇe ghoraṃ mucyate tatkṣaṇāj japan  RKS 
godānānna paraṃ dānaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam 
narmadāpayasi snātvā yo dadyād gāṃ dvijanmane  RKS 
saṃkhyāṃ kartuṃ yathāvac ca na devair api śakyate  RKS 
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe karmagatiyamavākyaṃ nāma catuṣpañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKS adhyāya 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
dhenuḥ katividhā proktā kasmin kāle ca dīyate 
sarvopaskarasaṃyuktā tvatta icchāmi veditum  RKS 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu rājan mahābāho kathyamānaṃ nibodha me 
kathayāmi tavākhyānam ādikalpe kṛte yuge  RKS 
cakravartī śaśāṅko 'bhūt sarvadharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ 
na ca varṇayituṃ śakyaḥ satyadharmavrate sthitaḥ  RKS 
bubhuje sa mahīmetāmekacchatrāṃ samāhitaḥ 
navakhaṇḍāṃ saptadvīpā yathā śakro 'marāvatīm  RKS 
hariścandrasya tasyāpi saṃvādaś cakravartinaḥ 
hariścandraḥ kurukṣetre gavām ayutam uttamam  RKS 
hemabhāramalaṅkārasarvaratnavibhūṣitam 
brahmarṣir mudgalo nāma svayaṃ brahma pratiṣṭhitaḥ  RKS 
mudgalāś ca dvijāḥ sarve satyadharmaparāyaṇāḥ 
śatamaṣṭottaraṃ sāgraṃ brāhmaṇā brahmavādinaḥ  RKS 
hariścandro dadau tebhyo rāhusūryasamāgame 
dvijān sampūjya vidhicchraddhayā parayā yutaḥ  RKS 
arcayitvā maheśānaṃ sthānaṃ paramasiddhidam 
cakrapāṇiṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ mudā paramayā yutaḥ  RKS 
sarasvatyāṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha tiladarbhānvitasya tu 
dānasyāsya prabhāveṇa lokāstenākhilā jitāḥ  RKS 
antarikṣe purī prāptā sarvalokamanoharā 
hariścandrapurī khyātā sā 'smil loke carācare  RKS 
satyadānasarvatyāgair ityādibhir alaṃkṛtaḥ 
hariścandrasamo rājā na bhūto na bhaviṣyati  RKS 
evaṃ gāthā purā gītā śakrādyaiḥ surasattamaiḥ 
śaśāṅko 'pyakarot sarvaṃ narmadātīramāśritaḥ  RKS 
dānaṃ yajña tapaḥ satyaṃ parvate 'marakaṇṭake 
dadau cārdhaprasūtāṃ brāhmaṇāya mahātmane  RKS 
dānasyāsya prabhāveṇa hariścandrādhiko 'bhavat 
anekabhāvikaṃ pāpaṃ dagdhvā tūlaughavacchikhī  RKS 
yāvad vatsasya pādau dvau mukhaṃ yonau pradṛśyate 
tāvad gauḥ pṛthivī jñeyā saśailavanakānanā  RKS 
svarṇaśṛṅgī raupyakhurī savatsā kāṃsyadohanā 
narmadāsnānayuktā tu sakuśā tilasaṃyutā  RKS 
oṃkārāmarayor madhye koṭitīrthe narādhipaḥ 
etāḥ sahasrasakhyātā brāhmaṇebhyo nyavedayat  RKS 
etasminn antare nedurdevadundubhayo divi 
tatkṣaṇād yānam ārūḍho jvalan maṇigaṇair iva  RKS 
stūyamānaḥ samīpasthair asaṃkhyātair vimānibhiḥ 
dhṛtasvarṇātapatras tu vījyamānas tu cāmaraiḥ  RKS 
yojanānāṃ sahasreṇa hariścandro 'py adhaḥ sthitaḥ 
tad dṛṣṭvā tādṛśaṃ karma śaśāṅkasya viśāmpateḥ  RKS 
sa vinindya kurukṣetraṃ vismayāviṣṭacetanaḥ 
mahānadyāṃ śaśāṅkena rāhusomasamāgame  RKS 
dattaṃ dānaṃ na sāmānyaṃ bhaved iti samāsataḥ 
viṣaṇṇavadano bhūtvā hariścandro nṛpottamaḥ  RKS 
brahmalokaṃ gataḥ kṣipraṃ yatra lokeśvaraḥ prabhuḥ 
abhivādya yathā nyāyaṃ papraccha sa pitāmaham  RKS 
dānena nirjitā devāḥ śaśāṅkena mahātmanā 
kiṃ ca puṇyamidaṃ brahman kurukṣetrād viśiṣyate  RKS 
amareśvaratīrthaṃ tu nāma revāsamudbhavam 
kenāpi na samaṃ bhūtam uparyupari dīpyate  RKS 
iti śrutvā vacas tasya hariścandrasya dhīmataḥ 
uvāca vacanaṃ brahmā hariścandraṃ nṛpottamam  RKS 
viṣādaṃ tyaja rājendra gahanā karmaṇāṃ gatiḥ 
śaśāṅkasadṛśo rājā na dṛṣṭo na śruto mayā  RKS 
evaṃ vaktuṃ na yogyo 'haṃ na devāpi savāsavāḥ 
anekāni sahasrāṇi purā vai cakravartinā  RKS 
iṣṭāni ca vidhānena parvate 'marakaṇṭake 
rāhusūryasamāyoge tīrthalakṣāṇi bhārata  RKS 
sarasvatīṃ kurukṣetraṃ puṣkaraṃ naimiṣaṃ tathā 
tīrthāny etāni cānyāni snānaṃ kartuṃ samāyayuḥ  RKS 
mekalāyāṃ hariścandra koṭitīrthe narādhipa 
tīrthānāṃ tyaja rājendra sāmyaṃ mekalayā saha  RKS 
vārāṇasyā kurukṣetraṃ tolitaṃ ca mayā purā 
tīrthāni na samaṃ yānti tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ  RKS 
khyātamātraṃ kurukṣetraṃ lokayātrāpravartakam 
purāṇaṃ na śrutaṃ yais tu mithyājñānasamanvitaiḥ  RKS 
sevyatāṃ kalpagā devī yadīcchet paramaṃ padam 
namaskṛtya vidhātāram ayodhyādhipatis tadā  RKS 
mudā paramayā yuktaḥ sa yayāv amareśvaram 
etat sarvaṃ samākhyātaṃ yathāvat tava suvrata  RKS 
yaḥ śṛṇoti naro rājan gosahasraphalaṃ labhet  RKS 
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe godānamahimānuvarṇano nāma pañcapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKS adhyāya 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
māhiṣmatyāḥ paścime vai tīrthaṃ pāpaharaṃ param 
aśokavanikā nāma sarvaśokavināśanam  RKS 
snātvā tatrārcayed gaurīṃ yathā vibhavavistaraiḥ 
mātaṅgasyāśrama tadvat siddhagandharvasevitam  RKS 
śuklakṛṣṇātṛtīyāyāṃ gandhadhūpavilepanaiḥ 
upahārair anekaiś ca dīpamālāprabodhanaiḥ  RKS 
tatra yā pūjayen nārī gaurīṃ bhaktisamanvitā 
rūpasaubhāgyasampannaṃ labhate satpatiṃ tu sā  RKS 
kārttikyāṃ tu gataprāṇā modamānā tu saṃyatā 
asya tīrthasya māhātmyāt prāptā māheśvaraṃ puram  RKS 
mātaṅgo nāma devarṣiḥ purākalpe yudhiṣṭhira 
narmadātīramāśritya tapas tepe suduṣkaram  RKS 
purā janmaniṣādaḥ sa jātiṃ smarati pūrvikām 
aghamarṣaṇadeśasthaḥ sarvadharma bubodha ca  RKS 
maharṣīṇāṃ prasaṅgena narmadādarśanena ca 
pāpabuddhiṃ parityajya dharmabuddhiṃ cakāra saḥ  RKS 
nirviṇṇo 'haṃ ca bhikṣuś cādhunā śvapacayoniṣu 
evam uktvā tato rājann aśokavanikāṃ gataḥ  RKS 
jaṭāvalkaladhārī ca kandamūlaphalāśanaḥ 
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu śivārādhanatatparaḥ  RKS 
śivadhyānaparaḥ so 'bhūd ugre tapasi saṃsthitaḥ 
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ hi tathā tasya tapasyataḥ  RKS 
ekāśītisahasrāṇi jaṭāgrebhyo viniḥsmṛtāḥ 
svayaṃ patanti vividhā narmadātoyam adhyataḥ  RKS 
tatkṣaṇād yakṣiṇīrūpā anantāś cāpramāṇikāḥ 
śyāmavarṇāḥ sutejaḥ kāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ  RKS 
yakṣalokaṃ vrajanty āśu tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ 
mantrayantravihīno 'pi śivabhaktiparāyaṇaḥ  RKS 
ṣaḍakṣaram imaṃ mantraṃ hṛdi cakre divāniśam 
oṃnamaḥ śivāya iti sarvamantrottamottamam  RKS 
tasya bhaktiṃ parāṃ jñātvā devadeva umāpatiḥ 
pratyakṣarūpo bhagavān chūlapāṇiḥ samāgataḥ  RKS 
uvāca vacanaṃ devo mātaṅgaṃ prati bhārata 
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te dhyānenānena suvrata  RKS 
mātaṅga uvāca
yadi tuṣṭo 'si deveśa varaṃ dātum ihecchasi 
mātaṅganāmnā vikhyātiṃ tīrtham etat prayātu vai  RKS 
cāṇḍālāḥ śvapacāś caiva pāpayonigatā 'pi 
japādi rahitāś cāpi mucyante 'trāpi kilbiṣāt  RKS 
mātaṅganāmaliṅgaṃ tu narmadātīram āśritam 
snātvā yo 'trārcayet tasya bhaved bandhavimokṣaṇam  RKS 
idaṃ varam ahaṃ manye tvatprasādāt maheśvara 
tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā praty uvāca śivāpatiḥ  RKS 
evam bhavatu tatsarvaṃ matprasādān na saṃśaya 
evam uktvā yayau deva kailāsaṃ parvatottamam  RKS 
varaṃ samprāpya mātaṅga umāmāheśvaraṃ puram 
kāmikaṃ yānam ārūḍhaḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣita  RKS 
jagāmāśu ciraṃ bhoktuṃ bhogān snānaprabhāvataḥ 
yā caitramāse 'māvāsyā kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśī  RKS 
tasyāṃ tatra hutaṃ dattam anantaphalam aśnute 
tilodakapradānena pāpayonigatā 'pi  RKS 
saktvāḍhyaguḍapiṇḍena pitṝn modayate tu yaḥ 
pitarastasya tṛpyanti yāvadindrāś caturdaśa  RKS 
tilataṇḍulamiśraṃ yaḥ kuryāl liṅgasya pūjanam 
so 'pi varṣasahasrāṇi śivaloke mahīyate  RKS 
aśokavanikā nāma mātaṅgaṃ tīrtham ucyate 
revāyā uttare kūle kathitaṃ tava bhārata  RKS 
athānyat kathayiṣyāmi yāmyabhāge vyavasthitam 
tīrthaṃ mṛgavanaṃ nāma sarvapāpapraṇāśanam  RKS 
tatra snātvā 'rcayed viṣṇuṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam 
ekādaśyāṃ mahārāja nirāhāro niśāṃ nayet  RKS 
hariṃ mṛgavane tatra gandhapuṣpaiś ca pūjayet 
ekasmin bhojite vipre lakṣaṃ bhavatu bhojitam  RKS 
tilodakapradānena pitṝṇāṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ padam 
tatraiva sanniviṣṭaṃ tu vārāhaṃ tīrthamuttamam  RKS 
yatra vārāharūpeṇa dharā caiva samuddhṛtā 
viśvarūpaṃ tathā cānyaddhariṇāmitatejasā  RKS 
pativratā ca nārī vai tathā māsopavāsinī 
tatra snātvā vidhānena lokaṃ prāpnoti vaiṣṇavam  RKS 
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe mātaṅgāśramavarṇano nāma ṣaṭpañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKS adhyāya 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
ākhyānaṃ kathayiṣyāmi khyātaṃ mṛgavanaṃ yathā 
vyādha kaścid durācāraḥ sarvabhūteṣu nirdayaḥ  RKS 
pāśahasto dhanuṣpāṇir vicaran girikandare 
ājaghāna mṛgān sarvān kuṭumbārthe nṛpottama  RKS 
jyeṣṭhe māsi tu saṃprāpte nidāghe jvalanaprabhe 
bhramati sma tṛṣārtaś ca vṛkṣamūle samāśritaḥ  RKS 
rātrau svapiti niśceṣṭo duḥkhārtaś ca kṣudhānvitaḥ 
vanasaṃgharṣajo vahnir utthito girikandarāt  RKS 
pradagdhaṃ ca vana tena mṛgavyāghrasamāvṛtam 
bhasmībhūtaṃ ca tatsarvaṃ reṇubhūtaṃ ca kṛtsnaśaḥ  RKS 
meghāgamoktakāle tu pravāhe nārmade śubhe 
kanyārāśigate bhānau dvādaśyāṃ śravaṇena tu  RKS 
narmadātoya saṃsargād yakṣā jātās tu pannagāḥ 
tatkṣaṇād divyadehās tu vaiṣṇavaṃ yānamāsthitāḥ  RKS 
sa vyādhaś cābhavad rājā tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ 
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi bhogān bhuṅkte manoharān  RKS 
ye 'pi dagdhā mṛgās tatra te 'pi gandharvatāṃ gatāḥ 
vaiṣṇavenaiva yānena prāptās tu vaiṣṇavaṃ padam  RKS 
avaśaḥ svavaśo vāpi yas tu prāṇān parityajet 
divyavarṣasahasraṃ tu viṣṇuloke sa modate  RKS 
tilodakapradānena pitṝṇāṃ paramā gatiḥ 
manorathaṃ nāma tīrtham anyat paramasiddhidam  RKS 
triṣu lokeṣu vikhyātaṃ revātīrasamudbhavam 
yaṃ yaṃ prārthayate kāmaṃ taṃ taṃ snātvāpi mānavaḥ  RKS 
sarva ca samavāpnoti tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ 
aṅgarāvartasaṃbhedo gosahasraphalapradaḥ  RKS 
aṅgāreśvaradevaś ca tatra tiṣṭhati saṅgame 
snānamātro naras tatra gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt  RKS 
aṅgāraś ca caturthyāṃ ca yadā bhavati bhārata 
hiraṇyapuruṣaṃ kṛtvā raktavastreṇa veṣṭayet  RKS 
ghṛtapūrṇaṃ tāmrapātraṃ guḍenāpi prapūritam 
tatsarvaṃ vidhivad dadyāc chrotriyāya viśeṣataḥ  RKS 
dānatīrthaprabhāveṇa śakrārddhāsanabhāg bhavet 
yasmāt pāpāni duḥkhāni tīvrāṇy api bahūnyapi  RKS 
tasmāt pāpaṃ na kartavyam ātmapīḍākaraṃ hi tat 
yasmin kāle ca deśe ca vayasā yādṛśena ca  RKS 
kṛtaṃ śubhāśūbhaṃ karma tat tathā tena bhujyate 
tasmāt sadaiva dātavyam avicchinna tayārthine  RKS 
vicchidyante 'nyathā bhogā grīṣme kusarito yathā 
saṃsevyate yathā devī saptakalpavahā śubhā  RKS 
saṃsārasya samucchittyai jñānayogaṃ bravīmi te 
śivaprakāśakaṃ jñānaṃ yogas tatraiva cintitaḥ  RKS 
durvijñeya gatir yogo narmadāśivasannidhau 
śivājñā vartate tatra snānapūjāvidhir yathā  RKS 
sa siddhāntā 'virodhena pustakair na virodhayet 
dharmajñānāpavargārthaṃ sahitaṃ vindate naraḥ  RKS 
pūrvottaravirodhena kutrārtho 'bhimato bhavet 
dṛṣṭvādyamūlatas tarkaṃ śrutyā saha vivarjayet  RKS 
tasmād āgamayuktena sadātmārthavicāraṇam 
kartavyaṃ nānumānena kevalena vipaścitā  RKS 
hīnottamādyasya phalaṃ bahudhā svaṃ ca tatsmṛtam 
tasmāt parīkṣāṃ kurvīta puṇyaṃ sādhu mahatphalam  RKS 
pākhaṇḍino vikarmasthān vaiḍālavratikāṃ śaṭhān 
varjayed dūrato dhīmān haitukyān tīrthanindakān  RKS 
digambarān śvetapaṭān ye cānye hetuvādinaḥ 
etaiḥ saha na saṃvādaṃ saṃsargaṃ na kathaṃcana  RKS 
viparītaṃ kalau dharmaṃ nagnā muṇḍā malāśinaḥ 
tasmāt taṃ ca parityajya tretādharmaṃ samācaret  RKS 
pramāṇaṃ sarvadharmeṣu brahmaviṣṇuśivoditam 
anyathā kurute yas tu narake patati dhruvam  RKS 
sarveṣām eva śāstrāṇām evaṃ śāstraviniścayaḥ 
sevyatāṃ kalpagā devī śivapūjārataiḥ sadā  RKS 
pitṝṇāṃ tarpaṇaṃ kuryād bhikṣāṃ dadyāc ca bhikṣave 
kāruṇyaṃ sarvabhūteṣu narmadākhyānacintanam  RKS 
idaṃ jñānamaśeṣaṃ ca sarvakarmaviśodhanam 
ādimadhyāntarahitaḥ svabhāvavimalaḥ prabhuḥ  RKS 
sarvajñaḥ paripūrṇaś ca śivo jñeyaḥ śivāgame 
sarvārthasādhakaṃ jñānaṃ tatpraṇītam asaṃśayam  RKS 
yaḥ sarvajñaḥ susampūrṇaḥ svabhāvavimalaḥ śivaḥ 
sarvadoṣavinirmuktaḥ sa brūyāt katham anyathā  RKS 
śivājñām antareṇāpi jagatsṛṣṭiḥ katham bhavet 
acaitanyāt pradhānena ajñatvāt puruṣasya ca  RKS 
pradhānaṃ paramāṇvādi yāvat kiṃcid acetanam 
tanna kartṛ svayaṃ draṣṭṛ buddhimatkaraṇaṃ vinā  RKS 
na yathā ghaṭam ānena mṛtpiṇḍaḥ svayam ṛcchati 
tathājñābuddhibhāvena na tiṣṭhet prakṛtiḥ svayam  RKS 
dharmādharmopadeśo na dharmādharmavicāraṇam 
sarvajñena vinā jātu nādisarge prasiddhyati  RKS 
yathānādi pravṛtto 'yaṃ ghoraḥ saṃsārasāgaraḥ 
śivo 'pi hi tathānādiḥ saṃsārān mocakaḥ smṛtaḥ  RKS 
vyādhīnāṃ bhaiṣajaṃ yadvat pratipakṣaṃ svabhāvataḥ 
tadvatsaṃsāraghorāṇāṃ pratipakṣaḥ śivaḥ smṛtaḥ  RKS 
vaidyaṃ vinā nirākrandāḥ kliśyante rogiṇo yathā 
śivena tu vinā sarvaṃ nirākrandaṃ jagat tathā  RKS 
tasmād anādiḥ sarvajñaḥ paripūrṇaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ 
asti nātaḥ paritrātā pumān saṃsārasāgare  RKS 
ye 'bhyasanti śivajñānaṃ hṛdaye śivabhāvitāḥ 
yadi vedāḥ pramāṇaṃ tu teṣāṃ jñānaṃ prajāyate  RKS 
iyaṃ ca sarvabhūtānāṃ śaraṇaṃ bhuvi narmadā 
apāṃ rūpatayā devī lokānugrahakāriṇī  RKS 
sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ caiva bhūtagrāmaṃ caturvidham 
bhagavaty uddharaty eṣāṃ patantaṃ narake dhruvam  RKS 
evaṃjñātvā naraśreṣṭha śivam anvīkṣya kalpagām 
uccairgṛhāṇi divyāni dhanadhānyānvitāni ca  RKS 
sarvopaskaradivyāni brāhmaṇebhyo nivedayet 
anāthāyātivṛddhāya vikalāya kuṭumbine  RKS 
kāṣṭhamṛnmayagehaṃ ca yo dvijāya prayacchati 
evaṃ vidhān gṛhān ramyān sarvato 'marakaṇṭake  RKS 
kārayed yaḥ pumān divyāṃs tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu 
kiṃ tasya bahubhir dattair dānair bhavati bhārata  RKS 
etad eva paraṃ dānaṃ sarvakāmārthasādhakam 
yaḥ śṛṇoti naro bhaktyā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  RKS 
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye saptapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKS adhyāya 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
śrutvaitat paramaṃ guhyaṃ gavāṃ devasam udbhavam 
brahmakūrcasya māhātmyaṃ śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥ  RKS 
ākhyāhi bhagavan sarvaṃ golokaḥ kīdṛśaḥ smṛtaḥ 
prāpyate karmaṇā kena ke tasminn aniśaṃ sthitāḥ  RKS 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śrūyatām abhidhāsyāmi namaskṛtya maheśvaram 
gomātṛlokaṃ paramaṃ sarvakām asamanvitam  RKS 
yathāvat sarvalokānām uparyupari saṃsthitam 
pātālāni tataḥ sapta pātālaṃ ca tatas tathā  RKS 
yāvat pramāṇaṃ paritaḥ paricchinnaṃ mahītalam 
tāvat pramāṇaṃ tasyāḥ samudrās tāni caiva tu  RKS 
teṣāṃ pratyekam utsedhapramāṇaṃ parikīrtitam 
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi daśārdhāni tatas tataḥ  RKS 
sahasrayojanotsedhas tasyābhyantaratas tathā 
vivarāṇāṃ samastānāṃ sahasrāṇi nava smṛtam  RKS 
teṣāṃ ruciramāhātmyaṃ nāmatas tu mahītale 
divyadivyopasampannaḥ śrīmaccāmīkaradyutiḥ  RKS 
nāgarājaḥ sadaivāste tasmin kṛtaniketanaḥ 
ananto 'nantadhāmā ca mukundo nṛpaśaivalaḥ  RKS 
tato rasātalaṃ nāma śivasantoṣabhūmikam 
vāsuker nāgarājasya tatra cāru mahāpuram  RKS 
pura ca suralomnas tu dānavādhipater mahat 
suparṇasya ca daityānām aśeṣāṇāṃ mahātmanām  RKS 
tataḥ sutalanāmāsti śarkarāñcitabhūmikam 
nāgādīnāṃ svastikānāṃ tatraiva vasatiḥ sadā  RKS 
dānavādhipatīnāṃ ca tatraiva nilayaḥ paraḥ 
vairocanahiraṇyākhyaprabhṛtīnāṃ mahātmanām  RKS

yatraiṣā narmadādevī plavantī lokatāriṇī  RKS

urvī kūrmatalākārā kāñcanī parimaṇḍalā  RKS

gandharvayakṣarakṣobhiḥ piśācaiś ca niṣevitaḥ  RKS

RKS adhyāya 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
dānadharmavidhānaṃ ca śrotum icchāmi kalpaga 
daridrā bhikṣavo vāpi kathaṃ yānti śivālayam  RKS 
vidhinā kena dānena mucyate duṣkṛtaṃ tathā 
lokānāṃ ca hitārthāya kathayasva mahāmune  RKS 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu rājan yathā nyāyaṃ kathayāmi tavānagha 
puṣkaraṃ bilvapatraṃ ca kuśāstoyaṃ ca nārmadam  RKS 
svayambhūr bhagavān āha sāmānyaṃ dharmakāraṇam 
śraddhāpūtāḥ sarvadharmāḥ purāṇaṃ śrutayas tathā  RKS 
tasyopadeśadharmeṇa narā yānti triviṣṭapam 
yas tūlapūrṇavistīrṇaṃ raktavastraṃ sasūtrakam  RKS 
vyāghracarmakṛtaṃ vāpi navavastrāvaguṇṭhitam 
kṛṣṇājinopavītaṃ ca puṇyadhūpādhivāsitam  RKS 
śivadhyānābhiyuktāya śraddhayā vinivedayet 
tat tūlavastratantūnāṃ romasaṃkhyāsti yāvatī  RKS 
tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi śivaloke mahīyate 
modate sarvalokeṣu bhuktvā bhogān anekaśaḥ  RKS

śivamuddiśya naivedyaṃ yo dadyāc chivadarśine  RKS

tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi śivaloke mahīyate 
bhikṣāṃ savyañjanāṃ dattvā śivabhaktāya bhaktitaḥ  RKS

dadhibhaktaṃ susampūrṇaṃ bhikṣāpātraṃ suśobhanam  RKS

sthitvā śivapure divye tasyānte ca mahīpatiḥ 
suśītalena toyena śivabhaktaṃ sitāyujā  RKS

dadyād yaḥ śivabhaktāya tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu 
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ vimānaṃ sarvakāmikam  RKS

palāśaparṇaiḥ patrair vā yaḥ kuryāt puṭakāni tu  RKS

yas tāmrapātraṃ sukṛtaṃ pradadyāc chivayogine  RKS

jñānayogabahiḥsthā ye lokasāmānyadharmiṇaḥ  RKS

sadehāś ca videhāś ca bhavanti svecchayā punaḥ  RKS 
iti nityaṃ viśuddhaṃ ca sthānam ādyam umāpateḥ

tataḥ kalpāyutasyānte sthānaṃ kaumāram āpnuyāt 
tatrārdhasammitaṃ kālaṃ sa krīḍan sasukhaṃ vaset  RKS 
tadante viṣṇulokaṃ ca saṃprāpya vasate punaḥ 
brahmalokaṃ gataś cānte tatrāpi vasate naraḥ  RKS 
brahmalokaparibhraṣṭo vasec chivapure sukham 
tat tasmād brahmaviṣṇvādyāṃl lokān prāpnoty anukramāt  RKS 
ity evaṃ sarvalokeṣu ramitvā kramaśas tataḥ 
manuṣyalokam āsādya śivaṃ revāṃ samāśrayet  RKS 
mayā te kathitā 'nyatra yāni dānāni bhārata 
tāni sarve praśaṃsanti parvate 'marakaṇṭake  RKS 
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye śivamahimānuvarṇano nāmaikonaṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKS adhyāya 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
vaiṣṇavaṃ dānadharmaṃ ca kathyamānaṃ nibodha me 
viṣṇuyogaṃ samabhyasya sarvakleśāpanuttaye  RKS 
viṣṇuṃ sampūjya vidhinā ghṛtasnānādibhiḥ stavaiḥ 
dvādaśyāṃ viṣṇum uddiśya dadyād ekāṃ payasvinīm  RKS 
narmadātīram āsādya tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu 
pūjyate dharmarājena yathā viṣṇus tathaiva saḥ  RKS 
śaivānāṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ ca sahasram bhojayet tu yaḥ 
garbhiṇī dhenusaṃmiśraṃ vṛṣabhair daśabhiryutam  RKS 
arcitaṃ gandhapuṣpādyair hemavastrair alaṃkṛtam 
pradakṣiṇam upākramya mantrarājaṃ ca bhaktitaḥ  RKS 
oṃ namo bhagavate vāsudevayeti samuccaran 
vedavidbhiḥ samākīrṇaṃ viṣṇor ārādhanaiḥ śubhaiḥ  RKS 
narmadātoyam āsādya dīpamālāṃ prabodhayet 
gāvo mamāgrato nityaṃ gāvaḥ pṛṣṭhata eva ca  RKS 
gāvo me hṛdaye vāpi gavāṃ madhye vasāmy aham 
imaṃ mantraṃ samutthāya japed āsāṃ puro gavām  RKS 
gandhato yākṣatair miśrair gṛhītvā tāmrabhājanam 
śṛṅgapuccha jalasnātaḥ śuklavastrasamanvitaḥ  RKS 
narmadāsnānapānena gavāṃ pucchāmbhasā tathā 
sarvakalmaṣanirmuktaḥ susiddhaḥ suciravrataḥ  RKS 
snāpayitvā gatas tatra sa vipro narmadātaṭe 
paurṇamāsyāṃ pūrṇacandre rāhusomasamāgame  RKS 
taireva sārddhaṃ viprendraiḥ saṃprapūjya hariṃ smaret 
bhṛtyaputrakalatrād yair yuktaḥ svajanabāndhavaiḥ  RKS 
nivedayet tu kṛṣṇāya mantreṇa śraddhayānvitaḥ 
śrāddhe dāne ca home ca vivāhe maṅgale tathā  RKS 
gomātaraḥ sthitā nityaṃ viṣṇuloke śivātmikāḥ 
śivāyaitā mayā dattā viṣṇave ca mahātmane  RKS 
evaṃ viprāya yo dadyād yajñārthaṃ samalaṃkṛtāḥ 
evaṃ nivedya puruṣo gosahasraphalaṃ labhet  RKS 
kulāni triṃśaduttārya narakād bhṛtyabāndhavān 
sthāpayed vaiṣṇave loke śivasya ca mahātmanaḥ  RKS 
sarvajñaḥ paripūrṇaś ca viśuddhaḥ sarvagaḥ prabhuḥ 
saṃsārasāgarān mukto haritulyaḥ prajāyate  RKS 
anenaiva vidhānena gṛhasthāḥ prāpnuyur divam 
vināpi jñānayogena gosahasrapradānataḥ  RKS 
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vāpi śūdro 'thāpi ca bhaktitaḥ 
narmadākapilāyoge yathā vibhavavistaraiḥ  RKS 
brāhmaṇāya daridrāya dīkṣitāyopaśobhine 
candrasūryoparāge tu vyatīpāte ca saṃkrame  RKS 
ṣaḍaśīti mukhe dadyād amāsomasamāgame 
kārttikyā vā yugādau vā puṇye vāhani bhārata  RKS 
yaddhi gāyanti pitaro gāthām etāṃ narādhipa 
api syāt sa kule 'smākaṃ putraḥ paramadhārmikaḥ  RKS 
narmadākapilāyoge koṭitīrthe ca muktide 
narakād uddhared asmān dattvā gā yas tu saṃyutāḥ  RKS 
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi loke krīḍati vaiṣṇave 
tasmāt tvam api rājendra gosahasraprado bhava  RKS 
devavad divi modante yena te pitaraḥ sadā 
kathayāmi tavāthāhamitihāsaṃ purātanam  RKS 
yuvanāśvaḥ purā rājā cakravartī mahāyaśāḥ 
śakrāc chatagaṇaṃ puṇyaṃ prajāpālanatatparaḥ  RKS 
ayodhyānagarī yasya brahmalokasamaprabhā 
tasyā kṛtayuge cādau sarvadharmaparāyaṇaḥ  RKS 
bṛhaspatibrahmasamaṃ vaśiṣṭhaṃ svapurohitam 
abhivādya yathānyāyam uvāca munisattamam  RKS 
kasmin sthāne yajed yajñaṃ tīrthe deśe surālaye 
vaśiṣṭhapramukhāḥ sarve munayaś cedam abruvan  RKS 
pṛthivyāṃ naimiṣaṃ tīrthaṃ sarvatīrthamayaṃ śubham 
saphalo hayamedhas tu koṭikoṭigaṇottaraḥ  RKS 
purāṇe kīrtitaṃ rājan matsyarūpeṇa viṣṇunā 
sūryeṇa kīrtitaṃ rājan manuputrāya cātmanaḥ  RKS 
sarveṣāṃ tu purāṇānāṃ purāṇaṃ matsyakīrtitam 
vedāścaiva purā naṣṭā matsyarūpeṇa coddhṛtāḥ  RKS 
vedahīnāś ca vartante dvijā vai yajñakarmasu 
evaṃ vidhaṃ tu tat tīrthaṃ yuvanāśva tavoditam  RKS 
evaṃ śrutvā tato vākyaṃ vaśiṣṭhasya purodhasaḥ 
ādideśa tato 'mātyān dharmiṣṭhān satyavādinaḥ  RKS 
yajñopaskaram ādāya samāgacchata satvaram 
ghoṣaṇā kriyatāṃ rāṣṭre daṇḍahastaiś ca kiṅkaraiḥ  RKS 
āhūtās tu tato devā nṛpater yajñakarmaṇi 
brahmā viṣṇuḥ sureśaś ca skando vaiśravaṇas tathā  RKS 
śambhuś caiva viśeṣeṇa surāsuranamaskṛtaḥ 
dhenūnāṃ daśalakṣāṇi hemaratnānvitāni ca  RKS 
lakṣamekaṃ hayānāṃ ca dantinām ayutatrayam 
maṇimāṇikyamuktāś ca hiraṇyaṃ cāpy anantakam  RKS 
nānāvidhāni dravyāṇi bhakṣyabhojyamalaṃkṛtam 
yajñadravyaṃ ca yac cānyat tat sarvasahito nṛpaḥ  RKS 
nānāsahasrayānais tu nānādeśagatair nṛpaiḥ 
nānāvādyasahasrais tu nānāgītair manoharaiḥ  RKS 
vedaghoṣeṇa mahatā divaṃ bhūmiṃ vinādayan 
viveśa naimiṣaṃ tīrthaṃ yatra devo maheśvaraḥ  RKS 
hariṃ sadyaḥ prabhuṃ dṛṣṭvā mucyate yatra kilbiṣāt 
svargasopānam etat tu pratyakṣaṃ devalokavat  RKS 
tatra snātvā 'bhyarcya hariṃ haraṃ svargam avāpnuyāt 
kīrtanān naimiṣasyāsya naro dahati tatkṣaṇāt  RKS 
anekabhāvikaṃ ghoraṃ tūlarāśim ivānalaḥ 
dīkṣitā brāhmaṇā devāḥ kutaścit tu samāgatāḥ  RKS 
ārtānām ayutaṃ tebhyo dadau devāya cānagha 
sahasram ekaṃ nṛpatirbhūṣaṇānāṃ ca bhārata  RKS 
oṃ namaḥ śaṅkarāyeti mādhavāyeti cottamaḥ 
jaladarbhau samādāya pātre rājā hiraṇmaye  RKS 
evaṃ saṃkalpya rājendra yajñavāṭam akārayat 
daśayojanaparyantaṃ yajñayūpāś ca hemajān  RKS 
tato nirvartito yajño vaśiṣṭhapramukhair dvijaiḥ 
muditā devatāḥ sarvā divyayānasamāśritāḥ  RKS 
jayaśabdaṃ pracakrus tā rājā nānyo bhavatsamaḥ 
nānyo mama samaḥ kaścid ityahaṃkāravān nṛpaḥ  RKS 
yāvad yānaṃ samāruhya sāntaḥpuraparicchadaḥ 
niḥsṛto naimiṣāraṇyāt tāvat paśyati vānaram  RKS 
tiṣṭha tiṣṭhety uvācātha śṛṇu rājan vaco mama 
kiṃ te yajñavidhānena devatādānakarmaṇi  RKS 
ahaṃkāravimūḍhātmā kartāham iti manyase 
purāmareśvare yajñe satyadharmasya bhūpateḥ  RKS 
varjayitvā mukham me 'bhūt kaṇṭhādho hemavarṇakam 
ye gatāḥ śiśavas teṣāṃ sarvāṅgāś ca hiraṇmayāḥ  RKS 
kapilā narmadāyoge yajñatoyapravāhataḥ 
snānāvagāhanāt pānāl loḍanāt kardame tathā  RKS 
gandharvalokaṃ samprāpto bhūtagrāmaś caturvidhaḥ 
tvadīye lulitaṃ yajñe naimiṣāraṇyasambhave  RKS 
paṅkena liptaṃ gātraṃ me kṣālitaṃ cāmbunā tathā 
na kiṃcit phalamāsīn me tava yajño nirarthakaḥ  RKS 
gavāṃ tvayāyute dattaṃ dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ tathā bahu 
bhūbhujā satyadharmeṇa kiṃtu tāvan nirarthakam  RKS 
dānena tapasā vāpi trayo lokāḥ samarjitāḥ 
sarveṣām eva tīrthānāṃ mātā vai mekalā smṛtā  RKS 
etat te kathitaṃ rājan yathābhūd amareśvare 
svasti vo 'stu gamiṣyāmi tvaṃ vāyodhyā prati vraja  RKS 
aham eva gamiṣyāmi narmadāṃ saptakalpagām 
śrutvā tvadīyaṃ yajñaṃ hi naimiṣāraṇyam āgataḥ  RKS 
nirāśo 'haṃ gamiṣyāmi nābhūn me kāṃcanaṃ mukham 
vānarasya vacaḥ śrutvā yuvanāśvo 'bravīd vacaḥ  RKS 
kastvaṃ vānararūpeṇa satyam etad bravīṣi me 
vānara uvāca
ahaṃ jābālinaḥ putraḥ kadambo nāma viśrutaḥ  RKS 
tiryagyonau praviṣṭaś ca prākṛtaiḥ karmabhiḥ svakaiḥ 
bhrāntāni sarvatīrthāni veṣeṇānena suvrata  RKS 
paritrāṇaṃ paraṃ nābhūt satyadharmamakhottame 
vapur hiraṇmayaṃ sarvaṃ mukhavarjaṃ mamābhavat  RKS 
vānarasya vacaṃ śrutvā sannivṛtya nṛpottamaḥ 
ārādhya devadeveśaṃ naimiṣe yajñapūruṣam  RKS 
uvāca vacanaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ praṇipatya prasādya ca 
madīyayajñe dānena tapasā niyamena ca  RKS 
śamicchaṃ chrāvayāmāsa eko vānararūpadhṛk 
hiraṇmayaṃ mukhaṃ cāsya yathā syāt tvaṃ tathā kuru  RKS 
uvāca vacanaṃ devo yuvanāśvaṃ mahīpatim 
pratyakṣaṃ naimiṣaṃ tīrthaṃ sūryakoṭisamaprabham  RKS 
pṛthivyāṃ naimiṣaṃ tīrtham antarikṣe ca puṣkaram 
triṣu lokeṣu vikhyāto giriś cāmarakaṇṭakaḥ  RKS 
na ca śrutaṃ tvayā tāta purāṇaṃ skandakīrtitam 
mātā sā yatra saritāṃ tīrthānāṃ ca saridvarā  RKS 
nāmasaṃkīrtanādasyā mucyate bhavabandhanāt 
viṣādaṃ tyaja tīrthānāṃ pradhāno 'marakaṇṭakaḥ  RKS 
satyadharmaḥ punas tatra kariṣyati makhottamam 
revākapilayor yoge mukhaṃ tatra hiraṇmayam  RKS 
bhaviṣyati na sandehas tava vānarasattama 
naimiṣaṃ sa namaskṛtya ādidevaṃ haraṃ harim  RKS 
sthānaṃ svaṃ ca jagāmātha mudā paramayā yutaḥ 
naimiṣasya vacaḥ śrutvā ayodhyādhipatis tathā  RKS 
viveśa nagarīṃ puṇyāṃ yathā śakro 'marāvatīm 
vānaro 'pi gatas tatra satyadharmo yataḥ svayam  RKS 
praṇamya satyadharmākhyam idaṃ vacanam abravīt 
revākapilayor yoge tvadīye ca mahāmakhe  RKS 
avabhṛthasnānajanite kardame luṭhanān mama 
śarīraṃ kāñcanībhūtaṃ mukham evāvaśiṣyate  RKS 
yajñamiṣṭvā punas tatra mukhaṃ me kāñcanaṃ kuru 
gandharvādhipatir bhūyo mukto vānarayonitaḥ  RKS 
hemībhūtavapus tatra yadā vānarasattamaḥ 
devandundubhinādena nānālaṅkārabhūṣitaḥ  RKS 
haṃsayuktena yānena vījyamāno 'psarogaṇaiḥ 
jagāma śāṅkaraṃ lokaṃ tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ  RKS 
tatra ye śvāpadās sarve te 'pi snātvā divaṅgatāḥ 
etat te kathitaṃ pārtha yathāvṛttaṃ purātanam  RKS 
śravaṇāt kīrtanāc cāsya gosahasraphalaṃ labhet  RKS 
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye ṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
śrutvā nānāvidhān dharmāstvatprasādān mahāmune 
nāhaṃ tṛptiṃ tu gacchāmi narmadākhyānakīrtanāt  RKS 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
gāvaḥ pavitramatulaṃ gāvaḥ sarvārthasādhakāḥ 
tasmāddhi gopradānena śivabhaktyā pramucyate  RKS 
yasmin deśe bhaven nityaṃ śivabhaktisamanvitaḥ 
so 'pi deśo bhavet pūtaḥ kiṃ punaś ca sabāndhavaḥ  RKS 
uktāni ṣaṭsahasrāṇi purāṇe mekalātaṭe 
ityāha jñānayogasya dharmayogasya tattvavit  RKS 
dharmādharmagatīnāṃ ca svarūpam upavarṇitam 
tīrthākhyānasamāyuktaṃ narmadākhyānam uttamam  RKS 
kīrtanāc chravaṇāt tasya mucyate bhavabandhanāt 
vidyāṃ siṃhāsane divye vastrapuṣpādhivāsitām  RKS 
pūjayitvā haraṃ viṣṇuṃ śṛṇuyād vācayet tathā 
śrīmatsiṃhāsanaṃ vāpi kḷptaṃ haimaṃ suśobhanam  RKS 
hemavastroparicchannaṃ nānāratnavibhūṣitam 
rājataṃ tāmrakaṃ kāṃsyaṃ brahmacārivinirmitam  RKS 
tat tu tārasamudbhūtaṃ śṛṅgavad ratnabhūṣitam 
divyaṃ siṃhāsanaṃ vāpi pūjāṃ kṛtvā prayatnataḥ  RKS 
gandhādhivasitakaraḥ śrīmadāsanasaṃsthitaḥ 
śambhvāyatanatīrtheṣu narendra bhavaneṣu ca  RKS 
bodhayet paramaṃ dharmaṃ gṛhagrāmapureṣu ca 
narmadākīrtanācchrotā śivaloke mahīyate  RKS 
idaṃ tīrtham idaṃ tīrthaṃ paryaṭan neti vai naraḥ 
narmadaiva paraṃ tīrtham ity āha bhagavān chivaḥ  RKS 
asmiṃstīrthe naraśreṣṭha śrāddhaṃ kāryaṃ vidhānataḥ 
svāgatena yamaḥ prītaś cāsanena śatakratuḥ  RKS 
pitaraḥ pādaśaucena atrādyena prajāpatiḥ 
viprapādodakaklinnā yāvat tiṣṭhati medinī  RKS 
tāvat puṣkarapātreṣu pibanti pitaro jalam 
vidyāvate snātakāya bhikṣave śrotriyāya ca  RKS 
tathā paramahaṃsāya viṣṇuvratadharāya ca 
sarvopaskaraṇaṃ dattvā śivaloke mahīyate  RKS 
anāhitāgniṃ yo vipram āhitāgniṃ karoti ca 
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ svavittenaiva kārayet  RKS 
ardhārdhaṃ saphalaṃ tasya yāvaj jīvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ 
viṣṇuloke 'ntakāle ca bhogān bhuṅkte ca puṣkalān  RKS 
svadravyeṇa ca yo yajñaṃ karoti vidhivad dvijaḥ 
narmadātīram āsādya brahmaloke sa modate  RKS 
dhātrīṃ hiraṇmayīṃ kṛtvā brāhmaṇāya prakalpayet 
kalpagā tīram āśritya viṣṇuloke mahīyate  RKS 
tilataṇḍulakarpūrasusambhojyavimiśritaiḥ 
kuṅkumair vastradhānyaiś ca nirmitaṃ śivasannidhau  RKS 
parvakāle ca yo dadyāt parvate mekalātaṭe 
vaset viṣṇulokeṣu naraḥ svarge na saṃśayaḥ  RKS 
pratyakṣadhenuṃ yo dadyāt hemaratnavibhūṣitām 
ghṛtadhenuṃ guḍadhenuṃ śarkarādhenum eva ca  RKS 
revākapilayor yoge dattvaitān narasattamaḥ 
sarvapāpavinirmukto loke krīḍati vaiṣṇave  RKS 
yadi tatra mahārāja bhikṣānnaṃ ca niveditam 
tasya saṃkhyā na vidyeta sa yāvat saṃgamo nṛpa  RKS 
etat sarvaṃ yathānyāyaṃ kathitaṃ tava suvrata 
vaivasvate 'ntare 'thānyac chṛṇu tvaṃ nṛpasattama  RKS 
vīraṇasya tu rājarṣer maitreyo 'bhūt purohitaḥ 
tena cāyatanaṃ viṣṇoḥ kāritaṃ narmadātaṭe  RKS 
puryāś caivāmarāvatyā diśi yāmyāṃ vyavasthitam 
tadāyatanamāhātmyān narmadāyāḥ prabhāvataḥ  RKS 
modate vaiṣṇave loke yugasyārddhaṃ dvijottamaḥ 
śṛṇu tvaṃ yāni tīrthāni revāyāḥ paścimottare  RKS 
vanaṃ meghavanaṃ nāma yajñaparvatam āśritam 
rantidevaḥ purā tatra cakravartī yudhiṣṭhira  RKS 
gavi nītaṃ kulaṃ yena sa devāsuramānuṣam 
pitaro mocitā yena gobhir vinihatāḥ purā  RKS 
cāṇḍālaiś ca hatā ye ca prāpnuvanti parāṃ gatim 
cāṇḍālād udakāt sarpād vidyuto brāhmaṇād api  RKS 
dantibhyaś ca paśubhyaś ca maraṇaṃ pāpaśālinām 
viṣṇor balipradānena kriyāṇāṃ karaṇena ca  RKS 
tīrthapiṇḍapradānena te yānti paramāṃ gatim 
dadhīcir nāma rājarṣir avantyadhipatis tathā  RKS 
sarvadharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ śakratulyaparākramaḥ 
purā devāsure yuddhe daityair devā vinirjitāḥ  RKS 
devānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ ca hantāro daityakaṇṭakāḥ 
naṣṭāḥ svapāpadoṣeṇa sabhṛtyakulabāndhavāḥ  RKS 
devāḥ samuditāḥ sarve lokapālāḥ savāsavāḥ 
nirvighnaṃ pṛthivīṃ kṛtvā lokaṃ caiva carācaram  RKS 
vindhyaṃ giriṃ gatās te tu yasmin vahati kalpagā 
samarthaṃ bhūpatiṃ jñātvā dadhīciṃ kurusattama  RKS 
dattāny astrāṇi rakṣārthaṃ tasya rājñaḥ surottamaiḥ 
vajraṃ śaktiṃ tathā pāśaṃ daṇḍaṃ khaḍgaṃ dhvajaṃ gadām  RKS 
triśūlaṃ ceti devānām āyudhāni pracakṣate 
tāni dattvā yathā nyāyaṃ nākapṛṣṭhaṃ mudā yayuḥ  RKS 
purāṇamatamājñāya dadhīciḥ satyavikramaḥ 
śāpasyaiva bhayād bhīto namaskṛtya pragṛhya ca  RKS 
prabhāvāt toyatāṃ nītvā śarīrāntar nyaveśayat 
tataḥ kālāntare prāpte dānavā baladarpitāḥ  RKS 
jambhakumbhahayagrīvapramukhāḥ punarutthitāḥ 
dānavānāṃ balaṃ jñātvā trastā devāḥ savāsavāḥ  RKS 
kāryakāle samutpanne saṃsmṛtyāstrāyudhāni ca 
nārada preṣayāmāsuḥ dadhīciṃ prati bhārata  RKS 
avantīṃ sa purīṃ prāpya devarṣir nāradas tathā 
viveśa bhavanaṃ rājño maṇikāñcanavedikam  RKS 
utthito nṛpaśārdūlo muniṃ dṛṣṭvā sutejasam 
pūjayitvā yathā nyāyaṃ hemakāsanasaṃsthitam  RKS 
taṃ tu dṛṣṭvā sukhāsīnaṃ rājā vacanam abravīt 
kim arthaṃ mānuṣe loke devalokāt samāgataḥ  RKS 
nārada uvāca
yuddhaṃ mahat samutpannaṃ devānāṃ dānavaiḥ saha 
samarpaya tvaṃ śastrāṇi kṣīyante dānavā yathā  RKS 
kuru kāryaṃ ca devānāṃ satyadharmavrate sthitaḥ 
dadhīcir uvāca
śṛṇu kāryaṃ ca devarṣe devānāṃ hitakāmyayā  RKS 
acireṇaiva kālena kṣayaṃ yāsyanti dānavāḥ 
mayā tāny eva śastrāṇi rakṣaṇārthaṃ mahāmune  RKS 
āpobhūtāni pītāni śarīre santi tāni vai 
upāyena hi gṛhṇantu dāsyāmy etāni vai punaḥ  RKS 
ityuktvā ca nṛpaśreṣṭha ājuhāva ca gāḥ purā 
māṃsādibhakṣitaṃ gobhir asthivarjaṃ viśāmpate  RKS 
astragrāmas tataḥ prāpto lokapālair yathā tathā 
gonardaṃ nāma nagaraṃ tat tu lokeṣu viśrutam  RKS 
dānavā nihatā devaiḥ punaḥ sṛṣṭiḥ pravartitā 
acintayat tadā tatra rantidevo mahīpatiḥ  RKS 
govidyutpaśucāṇḍālasarpairvinihatā narāḥ 
devalokaṃ na te yānti na teṣāmudakakriyā  RKS 
śocayitvā ciraṃ kālaṃ sāntaḥpuraparigrahaḥ 
prakṣālya narmadātoye tadasthīni vyasarjayat  RKS 
liṅgaṃ brahmeśvaraṃ tatra yajñaparvatasannidhau 
dharmasaṃśayam āpanno rantidevo mahīpatiḥ  RKS 
papraccha muniśārdūlān vaśiṣṭhapramukhān dvijān 
triḥpradakṣiṇam āvṛtya yathā nyāyam idaṃ vacaḥ  RKS 
ke deśāḥ parvatāḥ puṇyā nadyaḥ kāḥ kīrtitāḥ śubhāḥ 
narakasthān pitṝn yatra tadvadeyuḥ samuddharet  RKS 
akṣayaṃ ca pitṛśrāddhaṃ pitṝṇām akṣayā gatiḥ 
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
mārkaṇḍeyāśramaṃ gaccha asmābhiḥ saha bhūpate  RKS 
so 'pi sarvaṃ vijānīyāt kalpagā tīramāśritaḥ 
tac chrutvā rantidevo 'pi munibhiḥ paribhāṣitaḥ  RKS 
jagāma munibhiḥ sārddhaṃ kalpagātīravāsinam 
sa rājā brāhmaṇaiḥ sārddhaṃ praṇipatya tathā 'rcayat  RKS 
samutthāyābravīd vākyam upaviṣṭaḥ kuśāsane 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
kān na mocayate ghorān pitṝn saṃsārasāgarāt  RKS 
śṛṇvantu mama vākyāni munayo viditātmanaḥ 
sarvatīrthamayī revā sarvārthātmamayī śubhā  RKS 
śivenaitat nigaditaṃ purāṇe skandakīrtite 
kubjārevāsamāyoge viśeṣāt surapūjite  RKS 
tatra snātā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtā na punarbhavāḥ 
tatra śrāddhena yogena pitṝṇāṃ paramā gatiḥ  RKS 
idaṃ te kathitaṃ rājan kubjārevāsamāgame 
arcayitvā maheśānaṃ tatra bilvāmrakāhvayam  RKS 
sarvapāpavinirmukto gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt 
sārdhakoṭis tu kanyānāṃ tatra siddhiṃ parāṃ gatāḥ  RKS 
śaptāstāḥ pūrvamunibhiḥ kāmadoṣeṇa bhārata 
vidyādharāś ca yakṣāś ca gandharvāḥ kinnarās tathā  RKS 
śaptāstenaiva doṣeṇa kuberapuravāsinaḥ 
sarve te siddhim āpannāḥ kubjārevāsamāgame  RKS 
amāsomasamāyoge kārttikyāṃ caiva parvaṇi 
vārāṇasī prayāgaś ca puṣkaraṃ naimiṣaṃ tathā  RKS 
ete snātuṃ samāyānti kubjārevāsamāgame 
śravaṇāt kīrtanād asya śivaloke mahīyate  RKS 
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe rantidevopākhyānaṃ nāmaikaṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKS adhyāya 
rantideva uvāca
yathā śaptās tu tāḥ kanyās tāsāṃ nāmāni kalpaga 
śrotum icchāmi tattvena keṣu sthāneṣu pūjitā  RKS 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
vārāṇasyāṃ viśālākṣī naimiṣe liṅgadhāriṇī 
prayāge lalitādevī kāmukā gandhamādane  RKS 
mānase kumudā nāma viśvayonis tathāmbare 
gomante gomatī nāma mandare kāmacāriṇī  RKS 
madotkaṭā caitrarathe tapantī hastināpure 
kānyakubje tathā gaurī prabhā kamalaparvate  RKS 
ekāgre kīrtimatyākhyā viśvā viśveśvare tathā 
puṣkare puruhūteti kedāre mārgadāyinī  RKS 
nandā himavataḥ pṛṣṭhe gokarṇe bhadrakārṇikā 
sthāneśvare bhavānīti bilvake bilvapatrikā  RKS 
śrīśaile mādhavī nāma bhadrā bhadreśvare tathā 
jayā vārāhaśaile tu kamalā kamalālaye  RKS 
rudrakoṭyāṃ tu rudrāṇī koṭiḥ kālañjare tathā 
mahāliṅge tu kapilā mākoṭe mukuṭeśvarī  RKS 
śālagrāme mahādevī śivaliṅge jalapriyā 
māyāpuryāṃ kumārī tu santāne lalitā tathā  RKS 
utpalākhye sahasrākṣī hiraṇyākṣe mahotpalā 
tīrthāyāṃ maṅgalā nāma vimalā puruṣottame  RKS 
vipāśāyāmamoghākṣī pāṭalā puṇḍravardhane 
nārāyaṇī supārśve ca trikūṭe bhadrasundarī  RKS 
vipule vipulā nāma kalyāṇī pralayācale 
koṭīvikoṭi tīrthe tu yamunāyāṃ mṛgāvatī  RKS 
karavīre mahālakṣmīr umādevī vināyake 
ārogyā vaidyanāthe tu mahākāle maheśvarī  RKS 
abhayā kṛṣṇatīrthe tu amṛtā vindhyakandare 
māṇḍavye māṇḍukā nāma svāhā māheśvare pure  RKS 
chāgalambā pracaṇḍe ca caṇḍikā 'marakaṇṭake 
someśvare varāhī tu prabhāse puṣkarāvatī  RKS 
devamātā sarasvatyāṃ pārā pārāvate tathā 
mahālaye mahābhāgā payoṣṇyāṃ piṅgaleśvarī  RKS 
saṃhitā kṛtaśauce tu kārttikeye tu śāṅkarī 
utpalā varṣake lolā subhadrā śoṇasaṅgame  RKS 
mālāsiddhatale lakṣmīranantā bhāratāśrame 
jālandhare siddhamukhī tārā kiṣkindhaparvate  RKS 
devadāruvane puṣṭir medhā kaśmīramaṇḍale 
bhīmādevī himādrau tu tuṣṭir vastreśvare tathā  RKS 
kapālamocane siddhir mātā kāyāvarohaṇe 
śaṅkhoddhāre dhṛtir nāma dhvaniḥ piṇḍārake tathā  RKS 
kalā tu candrabhāgāyām akṣode śivadhāriṇī 
vaijayanty amṛtā nāma badaryām oṣadhī tathā  RKS 
oṣadhī cottarakurau kuśadvīpe kuśodakā 
manmathā himakūṭe tu pramate satyavādinī  RKS 
aśvatthe vandinī nāma nidhirvaiśravaṇe tathā 
gāyatrī vedavadane pārvatī śivasannidhau  RKS 
devaloke tathendrāṇī brahmaṇāsye sarasvatī 
sūryabimbe prabhā nāma mātṛkā vaiṣṇavī tathā  RKS 
arundhatī satīnāṃ ca apsarassu tilottamā 
citirbrahmakalā nāma śaktiḥ sarvaśarīriṇām  RKS 
etad uddeśataḥ proktaṃ nāmāṣṭaśatam uttamam 
aṣṭottaraṃ tu tīrthānāṃ śatam ekaṃ hy udāhṛtam  RKS 
yaḥ paṭhet prātarutthāya sa yāti paramāṃ gatim 
eṣu tīrtheṣu ye snātvā etāḥ paśyānti mānavāḥ  RKS 
sarvapāpavinirmuktās te yānti paramāṃ gatim 
yaḥ karoti tanutyāgam umāsthāneṣu mānavaḥ  RKS 
sa bhittvā brahmasadanaṃ padamāpnoti śāṅkaram 
nāmāṣṭakaśataṃ yas tu śrāvayec chivasannidhau  RKS 
tṛtīyāyāṃ tathāṣṭamyāṃ bahuputro bhaven naraḥ 
godāne śrāddhakāle ca vivāhe maṅgale tathā  RKS 
devārcanavidhau vāpi paṭhan brahmatvam āpnuyāt 
śrutvaitat stotramatulaṃ namaskṛtya ca parvatam  RKS 
rājā svapitṛmokṣāya yajñārthaṃ prāha kalpagam 
kasmiṃs tīrthe bhaved yajñaḥ pitṝṇāṃ mokṣadāyakaḥ  RKS 
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe mātṛstutirnāma dviṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKS adhyāya 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
revātaṭe mahāpuṇye pitṝṇāṃ mokṣaṇaṃ prati 
kuru yajñaṃ mahābhāga mucyante pitaro yathā  RKS 
iti śrutvā mahārāja namaskṛtya ca kalpagām 
vaśiṣṭhapramukhaiḥ sārddhaṃ jagāma svapuraṃ nṛpaḥ  RKS 
sa vatsānāṃ ca lakṣaikamaprasūtāyutaṃ tathā 
viṃśatiḥ śyāmakarṇānāṃ hayānāṃ ca daśāyutam  RKS 
maṇimāṇikyamuktādi bhūṣitoccaiḥ śravastviṣām 
ayutaṃ ca karīndrāṇāṃ ghaṇṭābharaṇaśobhinām  RKS 
maṇimāṇikyaratnānāṃ saṃkhyāṃ kartuṃ na śakyate 
nānādeśanṛpaiḥ sārddhaṃ brāhmaṇair vedapāragaiḥ  RKS 
veṇuvīṇāninādena brahmaghoṣaraveṇa ca 
āpūrayan diśaḥ sarvā divaṃ bhūmiṃ ca saṃspṛśan  RKS 
harṣeṇa mahatā yukto yajñasambhārasaṃvṛtaḥ 
rantidevo mahīpālaḥ kalpagātīram āśritaḥ  RKS 
anekabhakṣabhojyānāṃ tatra saṃkhyā na vidyate 
aṣṭayojanaparyantaṃ yajñayūpāś ca maṇḍapāḥ  RKS 
hemaratnamayāḥ stambhā maṇimauktikabhūṣitāḥ 
hiraṇmayāni kuṇḍāni vedikāś ca sahasraśaḥ  RKS 
sruvaś ca yajñapātrāṇi sarvaṃ svarṇam ayaṃ tathā 
samāhūtās tato devā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ  RKS 
candrādityau grahaiḥ sārddhaṃ nakṣatradhruvamaṇḍalam 
siddhā vidyādharā yakṣāḥ surāsuramahoragāḥ  RKS 
devarājaś ca devāś ca bṛhaspatipurogamāḥ 
tato yajñaḥ samārabdho brāhmaṇair vedapāragaiḥ  RKS 
homena tarpitā devāḥ sarvalokanivāsinaḥ 
nirdhūmaś ca jvalad vahṇiḥ saptajihvāsamanvitaḥ  RKS 
pratyakṣo havyavāhaś ca svayaṃ yajñe narādhipa 
tato nivartito yajño brāhmaṇair āptadakṣiṇaiḥ  RKS 
ghoṣaṇā bhrāmitā rāṣṭre pratīhāraiḥ sahasraśaḥ 
yo yaṃ kāmayate kāmaṃ so 'tra taṃ tvetyasaṃśayaḥ  RKS 
āhūtāḥ pūrvajās tatra mātṛkāḥ paitṛkās tathā 
apamṛtyuvaśaṃ prāptās tiryagyonigatāś ca ye  RKS 
te sarve śubhayonitvam āpannā yajñayogataḥ 
arcitā narmadādevīṃ pratyakṣā rūpadhāriṇī  RKS 
arcito bhagavāṃs tatra pārvatyā sahito haraḥ 
śrīpatiś ca śriyā sārddhaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ  RKS 
śakrādayas tathā devāḥ sapatnīkā alaṃkṛtāḥ 
gāścāśvāṃś ca karīndrāṃś ca brāhmaṇebhyo nyavedayat  RKS 
yac cānyad vidyate kiṃcid dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ payo dadhi 
agniśaucāni vastrāṇi sarvaṃ tebhyo nyavedayat  RKS 
yugapat pūjitā devā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ 
arcitā narmadādevī śailamūle vyavasthitā  RKS 
pravāho nirgato yatra kubjārevāsamāgame 
pitaras tarpitā devāḥ prāptāś ca paramāṃ gatim  RKS 
divyayānasamārūḍho dadhīciś ca nṛpottamaḥ 
śatamaṣṭottaraṃ pūrvaṃ paścimaṃ tad anantaram  RKS 
devayānapathe santaḥ śataśo 'tha nṛpottama 
ūcuś ca devās te sarve brahmādyā rantidevakam  RKS 
vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te prītāḥ satyenānena bhūmipa 
prāpto 'si paramaṃ lokaṃ pitṛbhir mātṛbhiḥ saha  RKS 
rantidevo 'bravīd vākyaṃ yūyaṃ me varadā yadi 
kalaśaḥ sthāpito yatra brāhmaṇair vedapāragaiḥ  RKS 
caturvedadharairbhaktaiḥ pañcabrahmatanuḥ svayam 
śivaliṅgaṃ bhavet tatra jvālāmālāsamaprabham  RKS 
yajñaparvatam āsādya pravāho yajñanirgataḥ 
snāne vinirgatā kubjā caruke carukā tathā  RKS 
carmilā cāṅghrimūle tu śilpe śilpā vinirgatā 
dhanado devatāś cānyāḥ sampūjya praṇipatya ca  RKS 
kalpagāṃ ca namaskṛtya kāmikaṃ yānam āśritāḥ 
stotraṃ cakre mahābhāga liṅgarūpasya śūlinaḥ  RKS 
lokanātho jagatsraṣṭā praṇipatya yathāvidhi 
brahmo vāca
nāsti rudrasamo devo nāsti rudrasamo guruḥ  RKS 
nityadāmalakāyāya svaprabhāmalamūrtaye 
śivabhasmāṅgarāgāya deveśāya namo 'stu te  RKS 
nīlakaṇṭhāya devāya sarvāyāmitamūrtaye 
bahurūpāya kāntāya śāśvatāya namo 'stu te  RKS 
parāya parameśāya sarvajñāya namo 'stu te 
sarvapraṇatadehāya svayam apraṇatāya ca  RKS 
pūjyānām api pūjyāya namastryakṣāya śūline 
brahmendraviṣṇuvedyāya utpattisthitihetave  RKS 
devastuta namaste 'stu bhuktimuktipradāya ca 
vāmāya vāmarūpāya vāmomāropabhāsine  RKS 
vāmakāntārdhavehāya īśānāya namo 'stu te 
śrutvā stotram idaṃ devo brahmaṇaḥ so 'mitadyutiḥ  RKS 
vṛṇīṣva vāñchitaṃ yajñe varam ity āha śaṅkaraḥ 
dadāmi te na sandeho yas tvayā vara īpsitaḥ  RKS 
uvāca vacanaṃ brahmā śaṅkaraṃ sarvagaṃ prabhum 
pañcavaktraṃ pañcaliṅgaṃ brahmapūjyaṃ prakīrtitam  RKS 
bilvā niveditā yasminn āmrāś ca viniveditāḥ 
bilvāmrakannāma liṅgaṃ saṃsārārṇavatāraṇam  RKS 
prasiddhiṃ paramāṃ yātu bhagavaṃs tvatprasādataḥ 
vāmanā mekalā yatra yatredaṃ liṅgam uttamam  RKS 
tatra snātvā naravyāghra śivalokam avāpyate 
idaṃ varam ahaṃ manye lokānugrahakārakam  RKS 
śaṅkaras tu tathety evaṃ prāha brahmāṇam avyayam 
evam uktvā maheśāno gaṇakoṭisamāvṛtaḥ  RKS 
stūyamānaḥ suraiḥ sarvaiḥ jagāma bhavanaṃ svakam 
brahmādyā devatāś caiva gatāḥ svaṃ svaṃ niveśanam  RKS 
rantidevaḥ pratuṣṭāva liṅgarūpadharaṃ śivam 
niśamya rantidevasya stotraṃ prāha maheśvaraḥ  RKS 
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te stotreṇānena suvrataṃ 
rantidevo 'bravīd vākyaṃ yadi me varadaḥ śivaḥ  RKS 
idaṃ tīrthaṃ na moktavyaṃ mahādeva sadā tvayā 
aghaughasamaplutā ye tu tiryagyonigatā narāḥ  RKS 
asya tīrthasya māhātmyāt te yāntu paramāṃ gatim 
atra yad dīyate dānaṃ sarvaṃ bhavati cākṣayam  RKS 
idaṃ varam ahaṃ manye yadi tuṣṭo 'si śaṅkara 
śaṅkara uvāca
amāsomasamāyoge kārttikyāṃ caiva parvaṇi  RKS 
atra yad dīyate dānaṃ tad anantaṃ samaśnute 
etat te kathitaṃ rājaṃs tīrthaṃ pāpapraṇāśanam  RKS 
viśvedevāḥ parāṃ siddhim asmiṃs tīrthe samāgatāḥ 
agastyaśaunakaś caiva parāśaro 'ghamarṣaṇaḥ  RKS 
saṃsiddhiṃ paramāṃ prāptā nānā munigaṇās tathā 
atrāyutaṃ munīnāṃ ca tapasā divamāruhat  RKS 
saṃkrame ca vyatīpāte grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ 
amāsomasamāyoge ṣaḍaśītimukhe tathā  RKS 
puṇyaṃ daśaguṇaṃ vṛddhiṃ satyam etac chivoditam 
sapādakoṭis tīrthānāṃ kubjārevāsamāgame  RKS 
dakṣiṇottarabhāge tu krośamātraṃ pratiṣṭhitam 
avaśaḥ svavaśo vā 'pi prāṇān yas tu parityajet  RKS 
rājā varṣasahasrāṇi vidyādharapure bhavet 
kṛmikīṭapataṅgādyās tīrthe 'smin prāṇamokṣaṇe  RKS 
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu rājā vidyādhare pure 
bilvāmrakaṃ siddhaliṅgaṃ kāmabhogaphalapradam  RKS 
kubjeśvaraṃ mahac cānyad brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati 
atrāntare mahārāja śivakṣetraṃ vidurbudhāḥ  RKS 
revākubjāsamāyoge yavānāṃ saptatistathā 
amāsomasamāyoge snānāc chāntiḥ prakīrtitā  RKS 
vārāṇasī kurukṣetraṃ prayāgo naimiṣaṃ tathā 
puṣkaraṃ ca gayā caiva kedāraṃ tīrtham uttamam  RKS 
phalam eteṣu sāmānyam amāsomasamāgame 
akṣayaṃ ca phalaṃ proktaṃ kubjārevāsamāgame  RKS 
tilodakapradānena mātṛkaṃ paitṛkaṃ sutaḥ 
narakād uddharet sarvān pūrvān api parān api  RKS 
so 'pi rājā gṛhaṃ prāptaḥ sarvān uddhṛtya pūrvajān 
ayaṃ te kathito rājan kubjārevāsamāgamaḥ  RKS 
rantidevo hariścandraḥ puruhūtaḥ purūravāḥ 
atreṣṭvā vividhair yajñair divyanti divi devavat  RKS 
śravaṇāt kīrtanād asya tīrthasya narasattama 
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā śivaloke mahīyate  RKS 
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe kubjāmāhātmye triṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
athānyat kathayiṣyāmi tīrthaṃ tīrthavaraṃ śubham 
yāmyapradeśe revāyā āśramaḥ surapūjitaḥ  RKS 
suvarṇadvīpapavikhyāto devadroṇīsamāvṛtaḥ 
hārīto gautamo viṣṇuḥ sāvarṇiḥ kauśikas tathā  RKS 
ete cānye ca bahavo munayaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ 
māsopavāsinaḥ kecid anye pakṣopavāsinaḥ  RKS 
cāndrāyaṇaparāś cānye tathānye kṛcchracāriṇaḥ 
phalamūlāśinaḥ kecit tathānye vāyubhakṣakāḥ  RKS 
kaṇadhūmaṃ pibanty anye jalāhārās tathā pare 
ekapādāḥ sthitāḥ kecid anye cārdhapadāḥ sthitāḥ  RKS 
dantolūkhalinaḥ kecidanye sūryāvalokinaḥ 
brāhmaṇāś ca brahmavidaḥ śrutismṛtiviśāradāḥ  RKS 
itihāsapurāṇāni mokṣopāyavicintakāḥ 
agnihotraparā nityaṃ japayajñakriyāparāḥ  RKS 
vedadhvanitanirghoṣais tārayanti jagattrayam 
na tasmin saṃcaret pāpaṃ tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā  RKS 
mekalādakṣiṇe tīre brahmaloka iva sthitaḥ 
āmrajambūkadambaiś ca kapitthair bilvadāḍimaiḥ  RKS 
kadalībījapūrādyair jambīraiḥ panasais tathā 
nyagrodhabadarair mukhyair bahuvṛkṣavibhūṣitam  RKS 
punnāgair nāgabakulair aśokais tilakais tathā 
mandāraiś campakaiś cāmrātakair nīlotpalotpalaiḥ  RKS 
patrapuṣpaphalopetair vṛkṣaiḥ sarvair alaṃkṛtam 
nānāpakṣigaṇopetaṃ siddhagandharvasevitam  RKS 
vyāharatyaṇḍajāḥ sarve mānuṣāṇāṃ girā nṛpa 
etad guṇasamāyuktaṃ suvarṇadvīpam uttamam  RKS 
svāyambhuve 'ntare rājann ādikalpe kṛte yuge 
arcanād devadevasya suvarṇadvīpavāsinaḥ  RKS 
apahāya tamaḥ kṛtsnaṃ loke krīḍanti śāṅkare 
pitṝṇām annadānena tilatoyapradānataḥ  RKS 
malāpakarṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā vasanti brahmaṇaḥ pure 
puṇyāyāṃ bhūpakārtikyāṃ sarvatīrthaphalapradaḥ  RKS 
naitat paśyanti manujāḥ kalau māyāvimohitāḥ 
kalpagā yāmyabhāge tu tīrthakoṭiranekadhā  RKS 
prasiddhaṃ siddhamunibhir jñāyate kevalaṃ hi tat 
nāstikair bhinnamaryādaiḥ purāṇasmṛtinindakaiḥ  RKS 
tailābhyaktair na vedoktakarai revātaṭe tathā 
kalimāyāvimūḍhaiś ca sthānaṃ tanna pradṛśyate  RKS 
hiraṇyagarbhāsthāne tu yasmin vahati kalpagā 
yajñagarbheśvaraṃ nāma śivaliṅgaṃ prakīrtitam  RKS 
pūjyate siddhagandharvaiḥ surāsuramahoragaiḥ 
yatra vaivasvato rājā sūryaputro mahāyaśāḥ  RKS 
tasya tīrthasya māhātmyāc candrabimbānano 'bhavat 
caitrasyaiva tu māsasya śuklapakṣe narādhipa  RKS 
caturdaśyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ yatra sannihito haraḥ 
tilodakapradānena piṇḍadānena bhārata  RKS 
pitṝn samuddharet tatra narakād bhūridakṣiṇaḥ 
nivased vaiṣṇave loke yāvac candrārkadarśanam  RKS 
tatra yaddīyate dānaṃ kurukṣetrasamaṃ hi tat 
prāṇatyāge kṛte tatra na paśyanti yamālayam  RKS 
revāyā uttare kūle paryaṅko nāma parvataḥ 
sa ca vindhyasutaḥ śrīmān sarvadevamayaḥ śubhaḥ  RKS 
tatra pāpaharo viṣṇuḥ svayaṃ tiṣṭhati keśavaḥ 
narapāpaharo yas tu narmadātaṭam āśritaḥ  RKS 
tatra snātvā mahārāja gosahasraphalaṃ labhet 
tarpitāḥ pitaras tasya tṛptā yānti hareḥ puram  RKS 
ekādaśīṃ dvādaśīṃ vā tatra yaḥ kurute naraḥ 
na tasya punarāvṛttir martyaloke durāsade  RKS 
krośamātrapramāṇaṃ ca harikṣetraṃ prakīrtitam 
apamṛtyumṛtā ye ca te yānti paramāṃ gatim  RKS 
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe viṣṇukīrtanaṃ nāma catuḥṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKS adhyāya 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
narmadāyāmyabhāge tu tīrthaṃ pāpapraṇāśanam 
māṇḍavyasyāśramaṃ puṇyaṃ siddhagandharvasevitam  RKS 
vibhāṇḍakaś ca gārgyaś ca ṛṣyaśṛṅgādayas tathā 
tasmin sahasrasaṃkhyātā munayaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ  RKS 
aśokavanikāṃ rājan chṛṇu sāmpratamuttamam 
tatra sannihito deva umayā sahito haraḥ  RKS 
āviṣṭaś cāśrame tatra viśoko vimalaḥ śivaḥ 
viśokayā saricchreṣṭhā narmadā yatra saṅgatā  RKS 
tatra snātā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtā na punarbhavāḥ 
aśokeśvaraliṅgam ca pratyakṣaṃ siddhiśaṅkaram  RKS 
śāpabhraṣṭā dvijās tatra nāradena vimocitāḥ 
tasya tīrthasya māhātmyāt modante divi devatāḥ  RKS 
nānāvṛkṣaphalaiḥ puṣpaiḥ sarvakāmasamanvitaiḥ 
nānā pakṣigaṇairjuṣṭaṃ nānāvṛkṣaniṣevitam  RKS 
siddhavidyādharair yakṣair gandharvaiḥ kinnarais tathā 
veṇuvīṇāninādena śaṅkhavāditraniḥsvanaiḥ  RKS

aśokā devatā yatra brahmaśakrapurogamāḥ  RKS 
viśvedevāśramaṃ taddhi sarvadevanamaskṛtam 
viśvāyāś ca tathā putrā viśvedevāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  RKS 
aśokavanikāyāṃ ca janayāmāsa kaśyapaḥ 
vaivasvate 'ntare prāpte tretāyāṃ narasattama  RKS 
pañcāyutāni tāni tīrthāni nivasanti śubhāni ca 
tatra siddhā ca sāvitrī devamātāditis tathā  RKS 
devayānī tathendrāṇī rohiṇī saṃbharāyaṇī 
dākṣāyaṇī lokavandyā lopāmudrā mahāyaśā  RKS 
ratnāvalī sūryabhāryā dhruvā tārā gaṇeśvarī 
aśokās tena vihitās tatrasthāḥ śatasaṃkhyakāḥ  RKS 
asya tīrthasya māhātmyān mucyate kilbiṣān naraḥ 
śuklapakṣe caturdaśyām āśvine māsi bhārata  RKS 
aputriṇī tathā bandhyā durbhagā bhartṛvarjitā 
pañcaratnaphalaiḥ snātā divyakumbhaiḥ samarcayet  RKS 
sahasrajanma sā bhūyaḥ putriṇī subhagā bhavet 
aśokavanikā kṣetre tatra gauryā varaḥ kṛtaḥ  RKS 
yasmin vahati sā devī narmadā saptakalpagā 
tatreṣṭaṃ dharmarājena varuṇena mahātmanā  RKS 
nairṛtyena tathānyaiś ca lokapālair yathā vidhi 
pratyakṣo havyavāhaś ca lokapālānupāgataḥ  RKS 
atrir marīciḥ kaśyapaś cakrus tatra makhottamam 
anyakṣetrāc chataguṇā tatra dānādikā kriyā  RKS 
vārāṇasī kurukṣetraṃ gayā vai naimiṣaṃ tathā 
māyāpurī puṣkaraṃ ca prayāgaḥ śaśibhūṣaṇam  RKS 
kāśyapī sarvatīrthāni yatra tiṣṭhati kalpagā 
aśokavanikāyās tu nānyat tīrthaṃ samaṃ viduḥ  RKS 
iṣṭaṃ yatra purā rājan hayamedhaṃ makhottamam 
brahmaṇā mocitāḥ pūrvaṃ viprāḥ kauleyayonitaḥ  RKS 
asya tīrthasya māhātmyāt pāṭalīputravāsinaḥ 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
hayamedhamakheneṣṭaṃ kathaṃ tāta svayambhuvā  RKS 
kathaṃ ca mocitā viprāḥ pūrvaṃ kauleyayonitaḥ 
ko vā rājā purā brahman devarājasamo 'bhavat  RKS 
etat sarvaṃ yathā nyāyaṃ śaṃsa me munisattama 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga samākhyānaṃ purātanam  RKS 
aśokavanikā tīrthaṃ kalpagā taṭamāśritam 
na jānanti mahāmūḍhā manujāḥ pāpamohitāḥ  RKS 
guptād guptataraṃ tīrthaṃ sarvatīrthottamottamam 
viśokeśvaraliṅgaṃ tu tasmin paramasiddhidam  RKS 
pūjyate siddhagandharvair na tat paśyanti mānuṣāḥ 
darśanāt sparśanāt tasya brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati  RKS 
svāyambhuve 'ntare prāpte ādikalpe kṛte yuge 
raviś candro mahārāja cakravartī mahāyaśāḥ  RKS 
somavaṃśe janiṃ prāptaḥ kāñcīpurapatis tathā 
śaśāsa pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ yathā śakras triviṣṭapam  RKS 
gatas tu pṛthivīpālo nānāvṛkṣasamākulam 
nānāpakṣigaṇairjuṣṭaṃ nānāmuniniṣevatam  RKS 
yatrāgastyeśvaraṃ nāma śambhorāyatanaṃ śubham

saptakalpavahā yatra śailaścāmarakaṇṭakaḥ  RKS 
hastyaśvarathapādātaiḥ sakośabalavāhanaiḥ 
tapasyantaṃ mahātmānaṃ munisaṅghaiḥ samāvṛtam  RKS

teṣāṃ madhye samutthāya śāṇḍilyaś ca mahātapāḥ  RKS

tvat pādārcanam ākāṅkṣī manyase ced anugrahaḥ  RKS 
agastya uvāca
āgacchatu nṛpaśreṣṭhaḥ śīghraṃ siṃhāsane sthitaḥ 
āgatas tad anujñātaḥ pādau jagrāha tasya ca  RKS 
arghapādyaiś ca sampūjya papraccha kuśalaṃ muniḥ 
kuśalaṃ te mahābhāga sāntaḥ puraparicchadaḥ  RKS 
uvāca vacanaṃ rājā munīndraṃ prati bhārata 
adya me saphalaṃ janma rājyaṃ jīvanam eva ca  RKS

yathā saṃsiddhyate yajñaḥ surāṇāṃ tṛptir akṣayā  RKS 
etat sarvaṃ yathā nyāyaṃ trikālajña nivedaya 
agastya uvāca
śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga kathyamānaṃ nibodha ca  RKS 
śivena kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ pārvatyāḥ ṣaṇmukhasya ca 
brahmaviṣṇvādidevānāmanyeṣāṃ ca divaukasām  RKS

tatte 'haṃ kathayiṣyāmi mekalātīrthasambhavam  RKS

kasya śaktir mahārāja varjayitvā maheśvaram  RKS 
pramāṇaṃ sarvatīrthānāṃ saṃkhyāṃ vā kartum āditaḥ 
uddeśamātravaktā 'haṃ mārkaṇḍasya mahāmuneḥ  RKS 
etat te kathitaṃ rājan yathāvṛttaṃ purātanam  RKS 
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye pañcaṣaṣṭitamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKS adhyāya 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
evaṃ śrutaṃ purā rājñā raviścandreṇa dhīmatā 
uvāca vacanaṃ śrīmānagastyo munisattama  RKS 
sarasvatī na gaṅgā ca yamunā vā na sāgarāḥ 
na caivānyāni tīrthāni prayāgapramukhāny api  RKS 
ekaiva narmadā puṇyā saptakalpavahā śubhā 
lakṣayojanaparyantaṃ jambūdvīpaṃ prakīrtitam  RKS 
narmadātoyapānena lokāloke carācare 
tapohīnā narāś caiva te 'pi yānti śivālayam  RKS 
yo 'yaṃ kāmayate kāmaṃ sa taṃ prāpnoti puṣkalam 
sādhu sādhu mahābhāga pṛṣṭo 'haṃ yat tvayānagha  RKS 
narmadā kathitā divyā hṛdyā kasya na rocate

tvatprītidāni tāvanti kathayāmi nṛpottama 
anyāni granthalakṣeṇa na ca kīrtayituṃ kṣamaḥ  RKS

siddhagandharvayakṣāś ca sakinnaramahoragāḥ  RKS

tatra siddhyati nirvighno yajña ity āha śaṅkaraḥ  RKS 
uvāca vacanaṃ rājā agastyaṃ munisattamam

viśvāmitro bharadvājaḥ kaśyapo bhārgavas tathā  RKS 
brahmadṛśyo lomaśaś ca tathānye munisattamāḥ 
vālakhilyā mahābhāgā mānasā brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ  RKS 
ete cānye ca bahavo munayaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ 
tataḥ pravartito yajño brāhmaṇair āptadakṣiṇaiḥ  RKS 
tṛptāś ca devatāḥ sarvāḥ pratijagmus triviṣṭapam

nātra vaivasvato nāhaṃ nāradaḥ parvatas tathā  RKS

āgatas tu yamas tatra nāradaḥ parvatas tathā  RKS

aśokeśvaradevasya narmadāyāḥ prasādataḥ  RKS

ekākī prārthaye nāhaṃ militvā prārthayāmahe  RKS

yo yaṃ kāmayate kāmaṃ taṃ tasmai pradadāmy aham

suprītā vihitā rājann arghapādyapradānataḥ

munayaḥ kena kāryeṇa pāṭalīputravāsinaḥ  RKS

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
purā tapodhanāḥ sarve jaṭāvalkaladhāriṇaḥ  RKS

pūjayanti śivaṃ bhaktyā gauryā virahitaṃ haram  RKS

saṃśaptās tena kāryeṇa pārvatyā liṅgabhedinaḥ  RKS

mudā paramayā yuktaḥ prāha tān prahasann iva  RKS

durvāsā uvāca

evamastviti tasyāgre 'bhidhāya munipuṅgavaḥ  RKS

prayāntu tvatprasādena dharmarāja śivālayam  RKS

yama uvāca
evaṃ bhavatu rājendra satyadharmaparāyaṇa  RKS

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
athātaḥ kathayiṣyāmi tīrthaṃ pāpapraṇāśanam 
revāyā uttare kūle puraṃ vāgīśvarābhidham  RKS 
vāgurnāma nadī tatra revayā saha saṃgatā 
tatra snātā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtā na punarbhavāḥ  RKS 
vāgīśā tatra cāmuṇḍā dānavakṣayakāriṇī 
maṇibhadro vīrabhadras tathā 'nye śataśo nṛpāḥ  RKS 
babhūvur muktaśāpās te tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ 
tilapiṇḍapradānena pitṝṇāṃ paramā gatiḥ  RKS 
brahmadattaścakravartī sūryavaṃśe mahīpatiḥ 
ayodhyādhipatiḥ śrīmān cakratulyaparākramaḥ  RKS 
dhanadhānyasamāyukto bhayadāridryavarjitaḥ 
prajās tasmin mahīpāle sarvā 'pi mudānvitāḥ  RKS 
iṣṭaḥ kratuvarastena narmadāvāgusaṅgame 
brahmādyā devatāḥ sarvāḥ śakraviṣṇupurogamāḥ  RKS 
pratyakṣaś ca maheśāno gaṇeśvarasamanvitaḥ

rāhusūryasamāyoge śuklatīrthe maheśvaraḥ 
candanāgurukarpūrapuṣpamālābhir arcitaḥ  RKS 
vitānadhvajamukhyaiś ca dīpamālāprabodhanaiḥ 
asya tīrthaprabhāveṇa yakṣarājo dhaneśvaraḥ  RKS 
bhogā nānāvidhās tena samprāptā divi devatāḥ 
sarvatīrtham ayaṃ tīrthaṃ sarvadevam ayaṃ ca yat  RKS 
api varṣasahasreṇa śuklatīrthasya varṇanam 
na śakyate suraiḥ kartuṃ purāṇe skandakīrtite  RKS 
pāpayonigato yaś ca tiryagyonigataś ca yaḥ 
brahmahā ca surāpaś ca śivanirmālyabhakṣakaḥ  RKS

tatra snānaṃ naraḥ kṛtvā pūjayitvā vṛṣadhvajam  RKS 
surāsuragaṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ pūjyate narasattama 
etat te kathitaṃ rājan mahāpātakanāśanam  RKS 
pitāmahena yatreṣṭo yajñe yajñeśvaraḥ purā 
stotraṃ kṛtvā yathā nyāyaṃ devadevasya śūlinaḥ  RKS 
pūjayitvā tu śukleśaṃ brahmā stotram udāharat 
namaḥ śivāya śāntāya jñānavijñānarūpiṇe  RKS 
sūkṣmāya sūkṣmarūpāya sarvasūkṣmāya hetave 
sūkṣmāṇām api sūkṣmāya namaḥ sūkṣmatamāya ca  RKS 
divyāya divyarūpāya divyadehāya setave 
divyānām api divyāya namo divyatamāya ca  RKS 
vyomaprabhāya bhāvāya aghorāya namo namaḥ 
vyomapramāṇadhāmāya vāmeśāya namo namaḥ  RKS 
parāya parameśāya pāramārthikahetave 
parāya paramuktāya namaḥ paratarāya ca  RKS 
ekajihvadvijahvāya bahujihvāya te namaḥ 
tathaivāsaṃkhyajihvāya triṇetrāya namo namaḥ  RKS 
pūjyāya pūjyapūjyāya sarvapūjyaikahetave 
nityāyānityarūpāya nityanityaikahetave  RKS 
nityānām api nityāya namo nityatamāya ca 
śaktāya śaktirūpāya sarvaśaktyekahetave  RKS 
śaktānām api śaktāya namaḥ śaktatamāya ca 
śuddhāya sarvaśuddhāya sarvaśuddhyekahetave  RKS 
kālāya kālarūpāya sarvakālaikahetave 
kālānām api kālāya namaḥ kālatamāya te  RKS 
sarvamantraśarīrāya sarvamantraikahetave 
mantrāṇām api mantrāya namo mantratamāya ca  RKS 
aprameyamaheśāya īśānāya namo namaḥ 
yogāya yogarūpāya yogapuruṣa te namaḥ  RKS 
ekakaṇṭhadvikaṇṭhāya bahukaṇṭhāya te namaḥ 
asaṃkhyakaṇṭhayuktāya nīlakaṇṭhāya te namaḥ  RKS 
anantāya maheśāya hartre kartre namo 'stu te 
namaste 'stu mahādeva namaste 'stu sadāśiva  RKS 
namaste 'stu mahāśuddha namas tubhyaṃ namo namaḥ 
namo bhasmāṅgarāgāya namaḥ khaṭvāṅgadhāriṇe  RKS 
sarvātmane namas tubhyaṃ viśveśāya namo namaḥ 
sarvajñāya namas tubhyaṃ sanāthāya namo namaḥ  RKS 
avyaktāya namas tubhyaṃ śāśvatāya namo namaḥ 
kailāsavāsine tubhyaṃ namaḥ pātālavāsine  RKS 
tvayā vyāptam idaṃ sarvaṃ lokālokaṃ carācaram 
api varṣasahasreṇa kaḥ stotuṃ śaktimān bhavet  RKS 
iti stavena divyena yaḥ stauti parameśvaram 
vidhūya sarvapāpāni rudraloke mahīyate  RKS 
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe śambhustutirnāmaikonasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kimarthaṃ saṃstuto devo brahmaṇā tena tatra vai 
śuklatīrtham idaṃ kasmādāste yatra maheśvaraḥ  RKS 
etat sarvaṃ samākhyāhi pṛcchato me mahāmune

śṛṇu rājan kathāṃ divyāṃ svargārhaṇyām anuttamām  RKS

yayātir uvāca

kedāraṃ bhairavaṃ caiva tathā rudramahālayam  RKS 
sarasvatīrudrakoṭiḥ prabhāsaṃ śaśibhūṣaṇam 
nānātīrthasahasreṣu dānayajñatapaḥ kṛtam  RKS 
etat te kathitaṃ sarvaṃ sūryaputramahāyaśaḥ 
anye dṛṣṭvā yathā nyāyaṃ dharmarājaṃ tatas tathā  RKS 
ūcuḥ sarve vacaḥ ślakṣṇaṃ dharmarājaṃ yathoditam 
na tvaṃ prabhuḥ sukṛtināṃ brahmā viṣṇuḥ śivaḥ prabhuḥ  RKS 
pāpakarmaratā ye tu teṣāṃ śāstā yamaḥ svayam 
yama uvāca
gatvā kailāsamāyāmi yāvat tāvat pratīkṣatām  RKS 
evam uktvā yayau rājan kailāsaṃ sa nagottamam 
yasmin śivādyās te sarve pārvatī ṣaṇmukhas tathā  RKS 
stuvanti devatāḥ sarvādevadevam umāpatim 
nṛtyanti cāgrataḥ kecid utpatya nipatanti ca  RKS 
taṃ dṛṣṭvā tādṛśaṃ śambhuṃ stuvantaṃ dīptatejasam 
stuvannāmasahasreṇa devadevaṃ pinākinam  RKS 
sāṣṭāṅgaṃ ca namaskṛtya dharmarājo 'bravīd idam 
ye 'smatpurīṃ samāyātās teṣāṃ kā gatir ucyate  RKS 
prahasann abravīd devo dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhira 
atra prayāntu te sarve ye revātīravāsinaḥ  RKS 
anyatīrthanivāsā ye bhogān bhuñjantu te divi 
śivavākyaṃ tataḥ śrutvā brahmāviṣṇur yathātatham  RKS 
tuṣṭā devasya vākyena sarvadevagaṇeśvaruḥ 
āgataḥ kṣaṇamātreṇa dharmarājaḥ purottamam  RKS 
śivoktāḥ preṣitāḥ sarve śivalokaṃ yudhiṣṭhira 
yathā yathā samādiṣṭās tato 'nye 'pi śūbhānvitāḥ  RKS 
purākalpe mayā dṛṣṭaṃ kārttikyāṃ devatāgame 
tato gacchen mahārāja vaiṣṇavaṃ tīrthamuttamam  RKS 
kokilā nāma vikhyātaṃ sarvapāpavimokṣaṇam 
vaiṣṇavaṃ kṣetramity āha devadevo janārdanaḥ  RKS 
sapādakoṭistīrthānāṃ tatrāste caiva bhārata 
upoṣyaikādaśīṃ puṇyāṃ dīpamālāṃ prabodhayet  RKS 
na tasya punarāvṛttir martyaloke durāsade 
sarvakāmasamṛddhena vimānāgreṇa bhārata  RKS 
asaṃkhyakālikā tṛptiḥ pitṝṇāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ 
vipre ca toṣite tatra dānasaṅkhyā na vidyate  RKS 
atrāntare tyajet prāṇānavaśaḥ svavaśo 'pi vā 
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi rājā vaidyādhare pure  RKS 
dhruvo dhruvatvaṃ svarge tu tārātejaḥ samujjvalan 
martyayoniṣu sambhūtā bhūtagrāmā tathāpare  RKS 
arcanrāḍ devadevasya divi devatvam āpnuvan 
devapuṇyakṣaye martyā bhaktyā puṇyaiś ca devatāḥ  RKS 
svargamartyaprabhedo 'yaṃ dharmādharmaprabhedataḥ 
kenāpi tatprakāreṇa pūjanīyo maheśvaraḥ  RKS 
yad vā tad vā śive deyaṃ bhaktiyuktena cetasā 
arundhatyā sā bharaṇyā sāvitryā ca tathā tathā  RKS 
ahalyayā menakayā marutvatyā ca rambhayā 
apsarogaṇasaṅghaiś ca surasiddhagaṇais tathā  RKS 
narmadātaṭam āśritya pūjito yena śaṅkaraḥ 
tena vai vipulā bhogāḥ prāptā mokṣaś ca bhārata  RKS 
na pūjayed dharaṃ yas tu śivamāyāvimohitaḥ 
na tasya svargamokṣau ca kailāsaṃ prati kā kathā  RKS 
na ca svargasya rājyasya bhājanaṃ ca narādhipa 
sarvatīrthamayī revā sarvadevamayo haraḥ  RKS 
sarvadharmamayī buddhiḥ kṣamāsatyam ayaṃ tapaḥ 
brahmacaryaṃ tapomūlaṃ pañcendriyavinigrahaḥ  RKS 
kṣamā satyaṃ japo 'dhītaṃ tapaḥ saṃyamalakṣaṇam 
etat te kathitaṃ rājaṃ śivena kathitaṃ purā  RKS 
mayā ca tava rājendra bhrātṝṇāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ 
na sāmānyatarā devī kathitā yā mayā tava  RKS 
dvīpeśvaraḥ kapileśvaras tathā vai narakeśvaraḥ 
etān devān samutthāya yathāvat parikīrtayet  RKS 
sarvatīrthaphalaṃ prāpya śivaloke mahīyate 
aghaughe ca parikṣīṇe prāpyate saptakalpagā  RKS 
śivaḥ saṃnihito yasyāṃ śivakṣetraṃ tataḥ param 
śravaṇāt kīrtanād asya śivaloke mahīyate  RKS 
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe dvīpeśvaravarṇano nāmaikasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKS adhyāya 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
narmadāsaṅgamaṃ puṇyaṃ surasiddhaniṣevitam 
tatra snātvā divaṃ yānti pūjayitvā maheśvaram  RKS 
āgacchantī purā loke narmadā bharatarṣabha 
stutā pūrvaṃ namaskṛtya devair brahmarṣibhis tathā  RKS 
tvayā pavitritaṃ puṇyaṃ martyalokaṃ carācaram 
apāṃ rūpagatā revā harasya paramā kalā  RKS 
umā kātyāyanī gaṅgā yamunā ca sarasvatī 
cāmuṇḍā carcikā devī revā tvaṃ saptakalpagā  RKS 
śivajā pravahā puṇyā mekalādrisutā stutā 
yajñayūpā ca mūrdhā ca svargamokṣapradā tathā  RKS 
tāriṇī sarvabhūtānāṃ pāpaghnī ca taraṅgiṇī 
lakṣmīḥ svāhā svadhā caiva puruhūtā yaśasvinī  RKS 
tvayā vyāptaṃ jagatkṛtsnam apāṃ rūpeṇa suvrate 
saṅgamaṃ siddhaliṅgaṃ ca surāsuranamaskṛtam  RKS 
atra dattaṃ hutaṃ sarvam etad bhavati cākṣayam 
atyadbhutaṃ mahārāja narmadāsnānam arcanam  RKS 
anekāni sahasrāṇi vimānāni yudhiṣṭhira 
nānāratnaprabhājālaiḥ sūryakoṭisamāni ca  RKS 
gatāni dharmarājasya purīṃ vīṇādiniḥ svanaiḥ 
nādayanti divaṃ bhūmiṃ vedanirghoṣaṇādibhiḥ  RKS 
ekasmin samaye dṛṣṭvāścaryaṃ vaivasvato nṛpaḥ 
atriś caiva vaśiṣṭhaś ca pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ  RKS 
ityādyāḥ sapta munayo dharmādharmavicārakāḥ 
śivena sthāpitāḥ pūrvaṃ hariṇā brahmaṇā tathā  RKS 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
akṣīṇakarmabandhus tu puruṣo munisattama 
paraṃ padam avāpnoti tan me kathaya kalpaga  RKS 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
viṣṇunā kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ brahmaṇe ca mahātmane 
prapadye puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim  RKS 
lokanāthaṃ sahasrākṣam akṣaraṃ paramaṃ padam 
bhagavantaṃ prapadye 'haṃ bhūtabhavyabhavatprabhum  RKS 
sraṣṭāraṃ sarvabhūtānām anantabalapauruṣam 
padmanābhaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ prapadye satyam avyayam  RKS 
hiraṇyagarbhaṃ bhūgarbham amṛtaṃ viśvatomukham 
anaśvaramanāthaṃ ca prapadye bhāskaradyutim  RKS 
sahasraśirasaṃ devaṃ vaikuṇṭhaṃ tārkṣyavāhanam 
prapadye sūkṣmam acalaṃ vareṇyam abhayapradam  RKS 
nārāyaṇaṃ hariṃ caiva yogātmānaṃ sanātanam 
śaraṇyaṃ sarvalokānāṃ prapadye dhruvamīśvaram  RKS 
yaḥ prabhuḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ yena sarvam idaṃ tatam 
yaḥ saṃhārakaro devaḥ sa me viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu  RKS 
yasmāj jātaḥ purā brahmā padmayoniḥ prajāpatiḥ 
prasīdatu sa me viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaparaḥ prabhuḥ  RKS 
purā laye tu saṃprāpte naṣṭe loke carācare 
ekas tiṣṭhati yogātmā sa me viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu  RKS 
jayed yaḥ pṛthivīṃ satyaṃ kālo dharmaḥ kriyāphalam 
gaṇākāraḥ sa tāṃ vāco vāsudevaḥ prasīdatu  RKS 
yogāvāsa namastubhyaṃ sarvāvāsa varaprada 
yajñabhogin pañcabhogin nārāyaṇa namo 'stu te  RKS 
caturmūrte jagaddhāma lakṣmīvāsa varaprada 
viśvāvāsa namaste 'stu sākṣībhūta jagatpate  RKS 
ajeyaḥ ṣaḍvibhāgaikaviśvamūrtir vṛṣākapiḥ 
mṛgādhipaś ca kālaś ca namas te jñānasāgara  RKS 
avyaktādaṇḍam utpannam avyaktād aparaḥ prabhuḥ 
yasmāt parataraṃ nāsti tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  RKS 
cintayanto hi yaṃ nityaṃ brahmeśānādayaḥ prabhum 
ekāṃśena jagatsarvaṃ yo viṣṭabhya vibhuḥ sthitaḥ  RKS 
agrāhyo nirguṇaḥ śāstā tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
divākarasya somasya madhye jyotir iva sthitam  RKS 
kṣetrajña iti yaṃ prāhuḥ sa mahātmā prasīdatu 
sāṃkhyayogena ye cānye siddhāś caiva maharṣayaḥ  RKS 
yaṃ viditvā vimucyante sa mahātmā prasīdatu 
namaste sarvatobhadra sarvato 'kṣiśiromukha  RKS 
nirvikāra namaste 'stu ādikalpa hṛdi sthita 
atīndriya namastubhyaṃ paramātman namo 'stu te  RKS 
ye ca tvām abhijānanti saṃsāre na vasanti te 
rāgadveṣavinirmuktā lobhamohavivārjitāḥ  RKS 
aśarīraḥ suguptaḥ san sarvadeheṣu tan mayaḥ 
avyaktabuddhy ahaṃkāramahābhūtendriyāṇi ca  RKS 
tvayi tāni na teṣu tvaṃ te ca tāni na tu svayam 
avyakto nātikūṭastho guṇānāṃ prabhurīśvaraḥ  RKS 
āvarto hetur ahitaḥ prabhuḥ svātmavyavasthitaḥ 
namaste puṇḍarīkākṣa vāsudeva namo 'stu te  RKS 
īśvaro 'si jagannātha kim ataḥ paramucyate 
bhaktānāṃ muktidas tvaṃ ca guruś ca tridaśeśvaraḥ  RKS 
same bhūtapatis tvaṃ hi prabhur janmani janmani 
ahaṃkāreṇa baddho vā tathā sattvādibhir gaṇaiḥ  RKS 
pṛthivīṃ yātu me ghrāṇaṃ yātu me rasanājalam 
cakṣurhutāśanaṃ yātu sparśo me yātu mārutam  RKS 
śabdaś cākāśam āyātu mano vai kāraṇaṃ tathā 
ahaṃkāraś ca me buddhiṃ tvayi buddhir mamāstv iti  RKS 
viyogaḥ sarvakaraṇair guṇair bhūtais tathā 'stu me 
sattvaṃ rajastamaś caiva prakṛtiṃ svāṃ viśantu me  RKS 
prabhoḥ prabhumanavadyaṃ prapadye 'haṃ naraḥ prabhum 
sahasraśirasaṃ devaṃ maharṣiṃ bhūtabhāvanam  RKS 
brahmayoniś ca viśvasya sa me viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu 
brahmapatnyāṃ pralīyante naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame  RKS 
āhūtasaṃplave caiva līyate prakṛtau mahat 
hūyate ca punas tābhyāṃ sa me viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu  RKS 
agnisomārkadevānāṃ brahmarudrendrayoginām 
yaste jayati tejāṃsi sa me viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu  RKS 
ajastvaṃ jagataḥ panthā amūrtirvīśvamūrtijit 
navaṃ pradhānaṃ ca mahān puruṣaś cetano 'lasaḥ  RKS 
agopyo yaḥ parataras tam eva śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
somasūryopamas tejo yo 'vatārayati svayam  RKS 
vijāyante diśo yasmāt sa mahātmā prasīdatu 
guṇavān nirguṇaś caiva cetano 'cetano svagaḥ  RKS 
sūkṣmaḥ sarvagato dehaḥ sa mahātmā prasīdatu 
sūryamadhye sthitaḥ somas tasya madhye tu saṃsmṛtaḥ  RKS 
bhūtatvād yo 'calo dīptaḥ sa mahātmā prasīdatu 
ekatvāt tava nānātvaṃ ye viduryānti te param  RKS 
samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu pradveṣyātmajanapriyaḥ 
samaṃ bhajaty anākāṅkṣī bhajate nānyacetasaḥ  RKS 
yo 'yaṃ sarvātmanā jñeyaḥ sa me viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu 
carācaram idaṃ sarvaṃ bhūtagrāmaṃ caturvidham  RKS 
tvayi taṃ tantuvat protaṃ sūtre maṇigaṇā iva 
na te dharmo hy adharmo 'sti na garbho janma vā punaḥ  RKS 
jarājanmavimokṣārthaṃ tam eva śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
indriyāṇi guṇaś caiva śvāsocchvāsaś ca yoniṣu  RKS 
kevalaṃ dāruvad dehaṃ naśyaṃ yat paramāpadam 
svayam ekākibhāvo me janmato 'tra punarbhavaḥ  RKS 
tvad buddhis tvad gataprāṇā tvad bhaktas tvat parāyaṇaḥ 
tvām evāhaṃ smariṣyāmi maraṇe paryupasthite  RKS 
pūrvadehe kṛtā ye tu vyādhayaḥ praviśantu mām 
vātādayaś ca duḥkhāni ṛṇaṃ tan muñcatāt prabho  RKS 
śreyasāṃ ca paraṃ śreyas tv anyeṣāṃ ca yaśasvinām 
sarvapāpaviśuddhyarthaṃ puṇyaṃ yatparamaṃ padam  RKS 
prātar utthāya satataṃ madhyāhne ca dinakṣaye 
ajasraṃ ca tathā japyaṃ sarvapāpopaśāntidam  RKS 
hariṃ kṛṣṇaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ vāsudevaṃ janārdanam 
praṇato 'smi jagannāthaṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu  RKS 
govardhanadharaṃ devaṃ gobrāhmaṇahite ratam 
praṇato 'smi gadāpāṇiṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu  RKS 
śaṅkhinaṃ cakriṇaṃ viṣṇuṃ śārṅgiṇaṃ madhusūdanam 
praṇato 'smi patiṃ lakṣmyāḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu  RKS 
dāmodaraṃ mudā yuktaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣam avyayam 
praṇato 'smi sthitaṃ sthityai sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu  RKS 
nārāyaṇaṃ naraṃ saumyaṃ mādhavaṃ ca janārdanam 
śrīvatsaṃ śrīvapuḥ śrīmac chrīdharaṃ śrīniketanam  RKS 
praṇato 'smi śriyaḥ kāntaṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu 
yam īśaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ dhyāyanti ca tamakṣaram  RKS 
vāsudevamanirdeśyaṃ tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
sarvabandhavinirmukto yaṃ praviśya punarbhavam  RKS 
puruṣo naiva prāpnoti tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
kṛtvā brahmavapuḥ sarvaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam  RKS 
yaḥ karoti punaḥ sṛṣṭiṃ tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
brahmarūpadharaṃ devaṃ yonirūpaṃ janārdanam  RKS 
sṛṣṭitve saṃsthitaṃ nityaṃ praṇato 'smi janārdanam 
yasmān nānyat paraṃ kiṃcid yasmin sarvam idaṃ jagat  RKS 
yaḥ sarvamadhyago 'nantaḥ sarvagaṃ taṃ namāmy aham 
yo 'sti bhūteṣu sarveṣu sthāvare jaṅgameṣu ca  RKS 
viṣṇur eva sa vai pāpaṃ mamāśeṣaṃ praṇaśyatu 
na vṛttaṃ nirvṛtaṃ karma viṣṇor yatkarma vā kṛtam  RKS 
anekajanmakarmotthaṃ pāpaṃ naśyati me tathā 
niśāyāṃ ca tathā prātar madhyāhṇe cāparāhṇayoḥ  RKS 
ajñānāc ca kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ karmaṇā manasā girā 
yatkṛtaṃ cāśubhaṃ kiṃcit tatsarvaṃ naśyatu kṣaṇāt  RKS 
tatsarvaṃ vilayaṃ yātu toyeṣu lavaṇaṃ yathā 
parapīḍāṃ ca nindāṃ ca kurvato janma nārjitam  RKS 
paradravyaparakṣetravāñchā krodhodbhavaṃ ca yat 
tatsarvaṃ vilayaṃ yātu toyeṣu lavaṇaṃ yathā  RKS 
viṣṇave vāsudevāya haraye keśavāya ca 
janārdanāya kṛṣṇāya namo bhūyo namo namaḥ  RKS 
nābhāgo nāma rājarṣir narmadātīrasaṅgame 
cakāra stotram atulaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tu prajāpatiḥ  RKS 
brahmaṇo 'ṅgirasā prāptaṃ tasmād indreṇa bhārata 
vaśiṣṭhaḥ śrāvayāmāsa nābhāgaṃ rājasattamam  RKS 
snātvā ca narmadātoye dattvā dānāny anekaśaḥ 
kāmikaṃ yānamāruhya nābhāgaḥ svapurīṃ yayau  RKS 
stauti nāmasahasreṇa yaḥ stavena janārdanam 
na tasya punarāvṛttirghore saṃsārasāgare  RKS 
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe viṣṇustutirnāma dvisaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ 
RKS adhyāya 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchec ca rājendra meghanādam iti smṛtam 
jalamadhye mahādevo yatra tiṣṭhaty adarśitaḥ  RKS 
yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
jalamadhye mahādevas tiṣṭhate kena hetunā 
uttaraṃ dakṣiṇaṃ kūlaṃ varjayitvā dvijottama  RKS 
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
etad ākhyānam atulaṃ puṇyaṃ śrutisukhāvaham 
purāṇe yacchrutaṃ tāta tat te vakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ  RKS 
purā tretāyuge tāta paulastyo devakaṇṭakaḥ 
trilokavijayī raudraḥ surāsurabhayaṃkaraḥ  RKS 
devadānavayakṣāṇāṃ gandharvoragarakṣasām 
avadhyo varadānena yatra paryaṭate mahīm  RKS 
tatra devagirau ramye dānavo baladarpitaḥ 
mayo nāmeti vikhyāto mahānāsīn nṛpeśvara  RKS 
rāvaṇas taṃ tato gatvā vinayāvanataḥ sthitaḥ 
pūjito dānasaṃmānair mayaṃ vacanam abravīt  RKS 
kasyeyaṃ padmapatrākṣī pūrṇacandranibhānanā 
kiṃ nāmadheyā tapate tapa ugraṃ kathaṃ vibho  RKS 
maya uvāca
dānavānāṃ patiḥ śreṣṭho mayo 'haṃ nāmanāmataḥ 
bhāryā tejavatī nāma mameyaṃ tanayā śubhā  RKS 
mandodarīti vikhyātā tapate patikāraṇāt 
śrutvā tu vacanaṃ tasya rāvaṇo madadarpitaḥ  RKS 
praśritaḥ praṇato bhūtvā mayaṃ vacanam abravīt 
paulastyo nāma rājāhaṃ devadānavadarpahā  RKS 
prārthayāmi mahābhāga sutāṃ tvaṃ dātum arhasi 
jñātvā paitāmahaṃ vaṃśaṃ mayenāpi mahātmanā  RKS 
sutā dattā rāvaṇāya kṛtvā vidhividhānataḥ 
gṛhītvā tāṃ tadā rakṣaḥ pūjyamāno niśācaraiḥ  RKS 
divyair yānair vimānaiś ca krīḍate tu tayā saha 
putraṃ putravatāṃ śreṣṭho janayāmāsa bhārata  RKS 
tenaiva jātamātreṇa ravo mukto mahātmanā 
saṃvartakasya meghasya yena loko jaḍīkṛtaḥ  RKS 
śrutvā tanninadaṃ ghoraṃ trasto lokapitāmahaḥ 
nāma cakre tadā tasya meghanādo bhaviṣyati  RKS 
etan nāmakṛtaṃ so 'pi paramaṃ vratam āsthitaḥ 
bhāvayāmāsa deveśam umayā saha śaṅkaram  RKS 
vratair niyamadānaiś ca homair jāpyairvidhānataḥ 
kṛcchracāndrāyaṇair divyaiḥ kliśyate ca kalevaram  RKS 
evam anyad dine tāta kailāsaṃ dharaṇīdharam 
gatvā liṅgam ayaṃ prāpya prasthito dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ  RKS 
narmadātaṭam āśritya snātukāmo mahābalaḥ 
nikṣipyāpūjayad devaṃ kṛtvā jāpyaṃ janeśvaraḥ  RKS 
gantukāmaḥ paraṃ mārgaṃ laṅkāyāṃ nṛpasattama 
ekaṃ samuddhṛtaṃ liṅgaṃ gṛhitaṃ savyapāṇinā  RKS 
prathamaṃ ca dvitīyaṃ ca bhaktyā paulastyanandanaḥ 
tadā devamahāliṅgaṃ patitaṃ narmadāmbhasi  RKS 
pāhi pāhīti tenokto liṅgena parameṣṭhinā 
dvitīyaṃ patitaṃ tāvad uttare narmadātaṭe  RKS

yāvad uddhartukāmo 'sau saptapātālam āgamat 
devayor niścayaṃ jñātvā nivṛtto 'sau niśācaraḥ  RKS 
jagāmākāśam āviśya pūjyamāno niśācaraiḥ 
tadā prabhṛti tattīrthaṃ meghanādeti viśrutam  RKS

pūrve tu garjanaṃ nāma sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram  RKS

ahorātroṣito bhūtvā sa labhecchāśvataṃ śubham  RKS 
piṇḍadānaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt tasmiṃs tīrthe narādhipa 
tena dvādaśa varṣāṇi pitaras tarpitā divi  RKS 
yas tu bhojayate viprāṃs tasmiṃs tīrthe narādhipa 
yatphalaṃ yogināṃ tatra labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ  RKS 
agniveśaṃ jale vāpi athavāpi hy anāśakam

śakra uvāca
narmadātaṭam āśritya toṣaya tvaṃ maheśvaram

brahmovāca

tvayoktaṃ vacanaṃ devi na caitad rocate priye
